### 30

<div class="d">
  A Psalm. A Song for the Dedication of the Temple. By David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V1">
    1
  </span>
  I will extol you, Yahweh, for you have raised me up,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and have not made my foes to rejoice over me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V2">
    2
  </span>
  Yahweh my God, I cried to you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and you have healed me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V3">
    3
  </span>
  Yahweh, you have brought up my soul from Sheol.
  <a href="#PSA30FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have kept me alive, that I should not go down to the pit.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V4">
    4
  </span>
  Sing praise to Yahweh, you saints of his.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Give thanks to his holy name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V5">
    5
  </span>
  For his anger is but for a moment.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His favor is for a lifetime.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Weeping may stay for the night,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but joy comes in the morning.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V6">
    6
  </span>
  As for me, I said in my prosperity,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “I shall never be moved.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V7">
    7
  </span>
  You, Yahweh, when you favored me, made my mountain stand strong;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but when you hid your face, I was troubled.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V8">
    8
  </span>
  I cried to you, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I made supplication to the Lord:
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V9">
    9
  </span>
  “What profit is there in my destruction, if I go down to the pit?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Shall the dust praise you?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Shall it declare your truth?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V10">
    10
  </span>
  Hear, Yahweh, and have mercy on me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh, be my helper.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V11">
    11
  </span>
  You have turned my mourning into dancing for me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have removed my sackcloth, and clothed me with gladness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA30V12">
    12
  </span>
  to the end that my heart may sing praise to you, and not be silent.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Yahweh my God, I will give thanks to you forever!
</div>
<div class="footnote">

    </span>

### 31

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V1">
    1
  </span>
  In you, Yahweh, I take refuge.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let me never be disappointed.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Deliver me in your righteousness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V2">
    2
  </span>
  Bow down your ear to me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Deliver me speedily.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Be to me a strong rock,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a house of defense to save me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V3">
    3
  </span>
  For you are my rock and my fortress,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  therefore for your name’s sake lead me and guide me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V4">
    4
  </span>
  Pluck me out of the net that they have laid secretly for me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you are my stronghold.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V5">
    5
  </span>
  Into your hand I commend my spirit.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You redeem me, Yahweh, God of truth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V6">
    6
  </span>
  I hate those who regard lying vanities,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but I trust in Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V7">
    7
  </span>
  I will be glad and rejoice in your loving kindness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you have seen my affliction.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have known my soul in adversities.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V8">
    8
  </span>
  You have not shut me up into the hand of the enemy.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have set my feet in a large place.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V9">
    9
  </span>
  Have mercy on me, Yahweh, for I am in distress.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My eye, my soul, and my body waste away with grief.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V10">
    10
  </span>
  For my life is spent with sorrow,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my years with sighing.
</div>
<div class="q">
  My strength fails because of my iniquity.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My bones are wasted away.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V11">
    11
  </span>
  Because of all my adversaries I have become utterly contemptible to my neighbors,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a horror to my acquaintances.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Those who saw me on the street fled from me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V12">
    12
  </span>
  I am forgotten from their hearts like a dead man.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I am like broken pottery.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V13">
    13
  </span>
  For I have heard the slander of many, terror on every side,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  while they conspire together against me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  they plot to take away my life.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V14">
    14
  </span>
  But I trust in you, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I said, “You are my God.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V15">
    15
  </span>
  My times are in your hand.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Deliver me from the hand of my enemies, and from those who persecute me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V16">
    16
  </span>
  Make your face to shine on your servant.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Save me in your loving kindness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V17">
    17
  </span>
  Let me not be disappointed, Yahweh, for I have called on you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the wicked be disappointed.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let them be silent in Sheol.
  <a href="#PSA31FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V18">
    18
  </span>
  Let the lying lips be mute,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  which speak against the righteous insolently, with pride and contempt.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V19">
    19
  </span>
  Oh how great is your goodness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  which you have laid up for those who fear you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  which you have worked for those who take refuge in you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  before the sons of men!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V20">
    20
  </span>
  In the shelter of your presence you will hide them from the plotting of man.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You will keep them secretly in a dwelling away from the strife of tongues.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V21">
    21
  </span>
  Praise be to Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for he has shown me his marvelous loving kindness in a strong city.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V22">
    22
  </span>
  As for me, I said in my haste, “I am cut off from before your eyes.”
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Nevertheless you heard the voice of my petitions when I cried to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V23">
    23
  </span>
  Oh love Yahweh, all you his saints!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh preserves the faithful,
</div>
<div class="q">
  and fully recompenses him who behaves arrogantly.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA31V24">
    24
  </span>
  Be strong, and let your heart take courage,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  all you who hope in Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
  <p class="f" id="PSA31FN1">
    <span class="notemark">
      †
    </span>
    <a class="notebackref" href="#PSA31V17">
      31:17
    </a>
    <span class="ft">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </p>
  <hr/>

### 32

<div class="d">
  By David. A contemplative psalm.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V1">
    1
  </span>
  Blessed is he whose disobedience is forgiven,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  whose sin is covered.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V2">
    2
  </span>
  Blessed is the man to whom Yahweh doesn’t impute iniquity,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in whose spirit there is no deceit.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V3">
    3
  </span>
  When I kept silence, my bones wasted away through my groaning all day long.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V4">
    4
  </span>
  For day and night your hand was heavy on me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My strength was sapped in the heat of summer.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V5">
    5
  </span>
  I acknowledged my sin to you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I didn’t hide my iniquity.
</div>
<div class="q">
  I said, I will confess my transgressions to Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and you forgave the iniquity of my sin.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V6">
    6
  </span>
  For this, let everyone who is godly pray to you in a time when you may be found.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Surely when the great waters overflow, they shall not reach to him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V7">
    7
  </span>
  You are my hiding place.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You will preserve me from trouble.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You will surround me with songs of deliverance.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V8">
    8
  </span>
  I will instruct you and teach you in the way which you shall go.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will counsel you with my eye on you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V9">
    9
  </span>
  Don’t be like the horse, or like the mule, which have no understanding,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who are controlled by bit and bridle, or else they will not come near to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V10">
    10
  </span>
  Many sorrows come to the wicked,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but loving kindness shall surround him who trusts in Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA32V11">
    11
  </span>
  Be glad in Yahweh, and rejoice, you righteous!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Shout for joy, all you who are upright in heart!
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 33

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V1">
    1
  </span>
  Rejoice in Yahweh, you righteous!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Praise is fitting for the upright.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V2">
    2
  </span>
  Give thanks to Yahweh with the lyre.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Sing praises to him with the harp of ten strings.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V3">
    3
  </span>
  Sing to him a new song.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Play skillfully with a shout of joy!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V4">
    4
  </span>
  For Yahweh’s word is right.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All his work is done in faithfulness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V5">
    5
  </span>
  He loves righteousness and justice.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The earth is full of the loving kindness of Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V6">
    6
  </span>
  By Yahweh’s word, the heavens were made:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  all their army by the breath of his mouth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V7">
    7
  </span>
  He gathers the waters of the sea together as a heap.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He lays up the deeps in storehouses.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V8">
    8
  </span>
  Let all the earth fear Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V9">
    9
  </span>
  For he spoke, and it was done.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He commanded, and it stood firm.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V10">
    10
  </span>
  Yahweh brings the counsel of the nations to nothing.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He makes the thoughts of the peoples to be of no effect.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V11">
    11
  </span>
  The counsel of Yahweh stands fast forever,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the thoughts of his heart to all generations.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V12">
    12
  </span>
  Blessed is the nation whose God is Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the people whom he has chosen for his own inheritance.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V13">
    13
  </span>
  Yahweh looks from heaven.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He sees all the sons of men.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V14">
    14
  </span>
  From the place of his habitation he looks out on all the inhabitants of the earth,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V15">
    15
  </span>
  he who fashions all of their hearts;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and he considers all of their works.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V16">
    16
  </span>
  There is no king saved by the multitude of an army.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  A mighty man is not delivered by great strength.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V17">
    17
  </span>
  A horse is a vain thing for safety,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither does he deliver any by his great power.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V18">
    18
  </span>
  Behold, Yahweh’s eye is on those who fear him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  on those who hope in his loving kindness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V19">
    19
  </span>
  to deliver their soul from death,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to keep them alive in famine.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V20">
    20
  </span>
  Our soul has waited for Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He is our help and our shield.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V21">
    21
  </span>
  For our heart rejoices in him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because we have trusted in his holy name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA33V22">
    22
  </span>
  Let your loving kindness be on us, Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  since we have hoped in you.
</div>

### 34

<div class="d">
  By David; when he pretended to be insane before Abimelech, who drove him away, and he departed.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V1">
    1
  </span>
  <a href="#PSA34FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Psalm 34 is an acrostic poem, with each verse starting with a letter of the alphabet (ordered from Alef to Tav).
    </span>
  </a>
  I will bless Yahweh at all times.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His praise will always be in my mouth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V2">
    2
  </span>
  My soul shall boast in Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The humble shall hear of it and be glad.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V3">
    3
  </span>
  Oh magnify Yahweh with me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let’s exalt his name together.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V4">
    4
  </span>
  I sought Yahweh, and he answered me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and delivered me from all my fears.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V5">
    5
  </span>
  They looked to him, and were radiant.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Their faces shall never be covered with shame.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V6">
    6
  </span>
  This poor man cried, and Yahweh heard him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and saved him out of all his troubles.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V7">
    7
  </span>
  Yahweh’s angel encamps around those who fear him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and delivers them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V8">
    8
  </span>
  Oh taste and see that Yahweh is good.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Blessed is the man who takes refuge in him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V9">
    9
  </span>
  Oh fear Yahweh, you his saints,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for there is no lack with those who fear him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V10">
    10
  </span>
  The young lions do lack, and suffer hunger,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but those who seek Yahweh shall not lack any good thing.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V11">
    11
  </span>
  Come, you children, listen to me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will teach you the fear of Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V12">
    12
  </span>
  Who is someone who desires life,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and loves many days, that he may see good?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V13">
    13
  </span>
  Keep your tongue from evil,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and your lips from speaking lies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V14">
    14
  </span>
  Depart from evil, and do good.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Seek peace, and pursue it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V15">
    15
  </span>
  Yahweh’s eyes are toward the righteous.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His ears listen to their cry.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V16">
    16
  </span>
  Yahweh’s face is against those who do evil,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to cut off their memory from the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V17">
    17
  </span>
  The righteous cry, and Yahweh hears,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and delivers them out of all their troubles.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V18">
    18
  </span>
  Yahweh is near to those who have a broken heart,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and saves those who have a crushed spirit.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V19">
    19
  </span>
  Many are the afflictions of the righteous,
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V20">

  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V21">

  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA34V22">
    22
  </span>
  Yahweh redeems the soul of his servants.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  None of those who take refuge in him shall be condemned.
</div>

### 35

<div class="d">
  By David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V1">
    1
  </span>
  Contend, Yahweh, with those who contend with me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Fight against those who fight against me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V2">
    2
  </span>
  Take hold of shield and buckler,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and stand up for my help.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V3">
    3
  </span>
  Brandish the spear and block those who pursue me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Tell my soul, “I am your salvation.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V4">
    4
  </span>
  Let those who seek after my soul be disappointed and brought to dishonor.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let those who plot my ruin be turned back and confounded.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V5">
    5
  </span>
  Let them be as chaff before the wind,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh’s angel driving them on.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V6">
    6
  </span>
  Let their way be dark and slippery,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh’s angel pursuing them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V7">
    7
  </span>
  For without cause they have hidden their net in a pit for me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Without cause they have dug a pit for my soul.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V8">
    8
  </span>
  Let destruction come on him unawares.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let his net that he has hidden catch himself.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let him fall into that destruction.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V9">
    9
  </span>
  My soul shall be joyful in Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  It shall rejoice in his salvation.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V10">
    10
  </span>
  All my bones shall say, “Yahweh, who is like you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who delivers the poor from him who is too strong for him;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  yes, the poor and the needy from him who robs him?”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V11">
    11
  </span>
  Unrighteous witnesses rise up.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They ask me about things that I don’t know about.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V12">
    12
  </span>
  They reward me evil for good,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to the bereaving of my soul.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V13">
    13
  </span>
  But as for me, when they were sick, my clothing was sackcloth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I afflicted my soul with fasting.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My prayer returned into my own bosom.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V14">
    14
  </span>
  I behaved myself as though it had been my friend or my brother.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I bowed down mourning, as one who mourns his mother.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V15">
    15
  </span>
  But in my adversity, they rejoiced, and gathered themselves together.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The attackers gathered themselves together against me, and I didn’t know it.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They tore at me, and didn’t cease.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V16">
    16
  </span>
  Like the profane mockers in feasts,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  they gnashed their teeth at me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V17">
    17
  </span>
  Lord, how long will you look on?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Rescue my soul from their destruction,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my precious life from the lions.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V18">
    18
  </span>
  I will give you thanks in the great assembly.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will praise you among many people.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V19">
    19
  </span>
  Don’t let those who are my enemies wrongfully rejoice over me;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither let those who hate me without a cause wink their eyes.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V20">
    20
  </span>
  For they don’t speak peace,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but they devise deceitful words against those who are quiet in the land.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V21">
    21
  </span>
  Yes, they opened their mouth wide against me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They said, “Aha! Aha! Our eye has seen it!”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V22">
    22
  </span>
  You have seen it, Yahweh. Don’t keep silent.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Lord, don’t be far from me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V23">
    23
  </span>
  Wake up! Rise up to defend me, my God!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My Lord, contend for me!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V24">
    24
  </span>
  Vindicate me, Yahweh my God, according to your righteousness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t let them gloat over me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V25">
    25
  </span>
  Don’t let them say in their heart, “Aha! That’s the way we want it!”
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t let them say, “We have swallowed him up!”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V26">
    26
  </span>
  Let them be disappointed and confounded together who rejoice at my calamity.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let them be clothed with shame and dishonor who magnify themselves against me.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V27">
    27
  </span>
  Let those who favor my righteous cause shout for joy and be glad.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yes, let them say continually, “May Yahweh be magnified,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who has pleasure in the prosperity of his servant!”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA35V28">
    28
  </span>
  My tongue shall talk about your righteousness and about your praise all day long.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 36

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. By David, the servant of Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V1">
    1
  </span>
  A revelation is within my heart about the disobedience of the wicked:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  There is no fear of God before his eyes.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V2">
    2
  </span>
  For he flatters himself in his own eyes,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  too much to detect and hate his sin.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V3">
    3
  </span>
  The words of his mouth are iniquity and deceit.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He has ceased to be wise and to do good.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V4">
    4
  </span>
  He plots iniquity on his bed.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He sets himself in a way that is not good.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He doesn’t abhor evil.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V5">
    5
  </span>
  Your loving kindness, Yahweh, is in the heavens.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your faithfulness reaches to the skies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V6">
    6
  </span>
  Your righteousness is like the mountains of God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your judgments are like a great deep.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh, you preserve man and animal.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V7">
    7
  </span>
  How precious is your loving kindness, God!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The children of men take refuge under the shadow of your wings.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V8">
    8
  </span>
  They shall be abundantly satisfied with the abundance of your house.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You will make them drink of the river of your pleasures.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V9">
    9
  </span>
  For with you is the spring of life.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In your light we will see light.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V10">
    10
  </span>
  Oh continue your loving kindness to those who know you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  your righteousness to the upright in heart.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V11">
    11
  </span>
  Don’t let the foot of pride come against me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t let the hand of the wicked drive me away.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA36V12">
    12
  </span>
  There the workers of iniquity are fallen.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They are thrust down, and shall not be able to rise.
</div>

### 37

<div class="d">
  By David.
</div>
<div class="q">

  <span class="verse" id="PSA37V13">

### 38

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by David, for a memorial.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V1">
    1
  </span>
  Yahweh, don’t rebuke me in your wrath,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither chasten me in your hot displeasure.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V2">
    2
  </span>
  For your arrows have pierced me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  your hand presses hard on me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V3">
    3
  </span>
  There is no soundness in my flesh because of your indignation,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither is there any health in my bones because of my sin.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V4">
    4
  </span>
  For my iniquities have gone over my head.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  As a heavy burden, they are too heavy for me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V5">
    5
  </span>
  My wounds are loathsome and corrupt
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because of my foolishness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V6">
    6
  </span>
  I am in pain and bowed down greatly.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I go mourning all day long.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V7">
    7
  </span>
  For my waist is filled with burning.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  There is no soundness in my flesh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V8">
    8
  </span>
  I am faint and severely bruised.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have groaned by reason of the anguish of my heart.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V9">
    9
  </span>
  Lord, all my desire is before you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My groaning is not hidden from you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V10">
    10
  </span>
  My heart throbs.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My strength fails me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  As for the light of my eyes, it has also left me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V11">
    11
  </span>
  My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my plague.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My kinsmen stand far away.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V12">
    12
  </span>
  They also who seek after my life lay snares.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Those who seek my hurt speak mischievous things,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and meditate deceits all day long.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V13">
    13
  </span>
  But I, as a deaf man, don’t hear.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I am as a mute man who doesn’t open his mouth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V14">
    14
  </span>
  Yes, I am as a man who doesn’t hear,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in whose mouth are no reproofs.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V15">
    15
  </span>
  For I hope in you, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You will answer, Lord my God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V16">
    16
  </span>
  For I said, “Don’t let them gloat over me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  or exalt themselves over me when my foot slips.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V17">
    17
  </span>
  For I am ready to fall.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My pain is continually before me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V18">
    18
  </span>
  For I will declare my iniquity.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will be sorry for my sin.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V19">
    19
  </span>
  But my enemies are vigorous and many.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Those who hate me without reason are numerous.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V20">
    20
  </span>
  They who render evil for good are also adversaries to me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because I follow what is good.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V21">
    21
  </span>
  Don’t forsake me, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My God, don’t be far from me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA38V22">
    22
  </span>
  Hurry to help me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Lord, my salvation.
</div>

### 39

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. For Jeduthun. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V1">
    1
  </span>
  I said, “I will watch my ways, so that I don’t sin with my tongue.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will keep my mouth with a bridle while the wicked is before me.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V2">
    2
  </span>
  I was mute with silence.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I held my peace, even from good.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My sorrow was stirred.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V3">
    3
  </span>
  My heart was hot within me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  While I meditated, the fire burned.
</div>
<div class="q">
  I spoke with my tongue:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V4">
    4
  </span>
  “Yahweh, show me my end,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  what is the measure of my days.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let me know how frail I am.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V5">
    5
  </span>
  Behold, you have made my days hand widths.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My lifetime is as nothing before you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Surely every man stands as a breath.”
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V6">
    6
  </span>
  “Surely every man walks like a shadow.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Surely they busy themselves in vain.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He heaps up, and doesn’t know who shall gather.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V7">
    7
  </span>
  Now, Lord, what do I wait for?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My hope is in you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V8">
    8
  </span>
  Deliver me from all my transgressions.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t make me the reproach of the foolish.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V9">
    9
  </span>
  I was mute.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I didn’t open my mouth,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because you did it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V10">
    10
  </span>
  Remove your scourge away from me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I am overcome by the blow of your hand.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V11">
    11
  </span>
  When you rebuke and correct man for iniquity,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  you consume his wealth like a moth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Surely every man is but a breath.”
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V12">
    12
  </span>
  “Hear my prayer, Yahweh, and give ear to my cry.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t be silent at my tears.
</div>
<div class="q">
  For I am a stranger with you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a foreigner, as all my fathers were.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA39V13">
    13
  </span>
  Oh spare me, that I may recover strength,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  before I go away and exist no more.”
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 40

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V1">
    1
  </span>
  I waited patiently for Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He turned to me, and heard my cry.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V2">
    2
  </span>
  He brought me up also out of a horrible pit,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  out of the miry clay.
</div>
<div class="q">
  He set my feet on a rock,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and gave me a firm place to stand.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V3">
    3
  </span>
  He has put a new song in my mouth, even praise to our God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Many shall see it, and fear, and shall trust in Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V4">
    4
  </span>
  Blessed is the man who makes Yahweh his trust,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and doesn’t respect the proud, nor such as turn away to lies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V5">
    5
  </span>
  Many, Yahweh, my God, are the wonderful works which you have done,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and your thoughts which are toward us.
</div>
<div class="q">
  They can’t be declared back to you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  If I would declare and speak of them, they are more than can be counted.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V6">
    6
  </span>
  Sacrifice and offering you didn’t desire.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have opened my ears.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have not required burnt offering and sin offering.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V7">
    7
  </span>
  Then I said, “Behold, I have come.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  It is written about me in the book in the scroll.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V8">
    8
  </span>
  I delight to do your will, my God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yes, your law is within my heart.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V9">
    9
  </span>
  I have proclaimed glad news of righteousness in the great assembly.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Behold, I will not seal my lips, Yahweh, you know.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V10">
    10
  </span>
  I have not hidden your righteousness within my heart.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have declared your faithfulness and your salvation.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have not concealed your loving kindness and your truth from the great assembly.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V11">
    11
  </span>
  Don’t withhold your tender mercies from me, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let your loving kindness and your truth continually preserve me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V12">
    12
  </span>
  For innumerable evils have surrounded me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My iniquities have overtaken me, so that I am not able to look up.
</div>
<div class="q">
  They are more than the hairs of my head.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My heart has failed me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V13">
    13
  </span>
  Be pleased, Yahweh, to deliver me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Hurry to help me, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V14">
    14
  </span>
  Let them be disappointed and confounded together who seek after my soul to destroy it.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let them be turned backward and brought to dishonor who delight in my hurt.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V15">
    15
  </span>
  Let them be desolate by reason of their shame that tell me, “Aha! Aha!”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V16">
    16
  </span>
  Let all those who seek you rejoice and be glad in you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let such as love your salvation say continually, “Let Yahweh be exalted!”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA40V17">
    17
  </span>
  But I am poor and needy.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  May the Lord think about me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  You are my help and my deliverer.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t delay, my God.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>

### 41

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V1">
    1
  </span>
  Blessed is he who considers the poor.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh will deliver him in the day of evil.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V2">
    2
  </span>
  Yahweh will preserve him, and keep him alive.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He shall be blessed on the earth,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and he will not surrender him to the will of his enemies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V3">
    3
  </span>
  Yahweh will sustain him on his sickbed,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and restore him from his bed of illness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V4">
    4
  </span>
  I said, “Yahweh, have mercy on me!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Heal me, for I have sinned against you.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V5">
    5
  </span>
  My enemies speak evil against me:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “When will he die, and his name perish?”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V6">
    6
  </span>
  If he comes to see me, he speaks falsehood.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His heart gathers iniquity to itself.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  When he goes abroad, he tells it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V7">
    7
  </span>
  All who hate me whisper together against me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They imagine the worst for me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V8">
    8
  </span>
  “An evil disease”, they say, “has afflicted him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Now that he lies he shall rise up no more.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V9">
    9
  </span>
  Yes, my own familiar friend, in whom I trusted,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who ate bread with me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  has lifted up his heel against me.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V10">
    10
  </span>
  But you, Yahweh, have mercy on me, and raise me up,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that I may repay them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V11">
    11
  </span>
  By this I know that you delight in me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because my enemy doesn’t triumph over me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V12">
    12
  </span>
  As for me, you uphold me in my integrity,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and set me in your presence forever.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA41V13">
    13
  </span>
  Blessed be Yahweh, the God of Israel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  from everlasting and to everlasting!
</div>
<div class="q">
  Amen and amen.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>

### 42

<div class="ms">
  BOOK 2
</div>
<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A contemplation by the sons of Korah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V1">
    1
  </span>
  As the deer pants for the water brooks,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so my soul pants after you, God.
  <a href="#PSA42FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      The Hebrew word rendered “God” is “אֱלֹהִ֑ים” (Elohim).
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V2">
    2
  </span>
  My soul thirsts for God, for the living God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  When shall I come and appear before God?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V3">
    3
  </span>
  My tears have been my food day and night,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  while they continually ask me, “Where is your God?”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V4">
    4
  </span>
  These things I remember, and pour out my soul within me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  how I used to go with the crowd, and led them to God’s house,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  with the voice of joy and praise, a multitude keeping a holy day.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V5">
    5
  </span>
  Why are you in despair, my soul?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Why are you disturbed within me?
</div>
<div class="q">
  Hope in God!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  For I shall still praise him for the saving help of his presence.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V6">
    6
  </span>
  My God, my soul is in despair within me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Therefore I remember you from the land of the Jordan,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the heights of Hermon, from the hill Mizar.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V7">
    7
  </span>
  Deep calls to deep at the noise of your waterfalls.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All your waves and your billows have swept over me.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V8">
    8
  </span>
  Yahweh
  <a href="#PSA42FN2" class="notemark">
    ‡
    <span class="popup">
      “Yahweh” is God’s proper Name, sometimes rendered “LORD” (all caps) in other translations.
    </span>
  </a>
  will command his loving kindness in the daytime.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In the night his song shall be with me:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a prayer to the God of my life.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V9">
    9
  </span>
  I will ask God, my rock, “Why have you forgotten me?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Why do I go mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V10">
    10
  </span>
  As with a sword in my bones, my adversaries reproach me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  while they continually ask me, “Where is your God?”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA42V11">
    11
  </span>
  Why are you in despair, my soul?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Why are you disturbed within me?
</div>
<div class="q">
  Hope in God! For I shall still praise him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the saving help of my countenance, and my God.

### 44

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. By the sons of Korah. A contemplative psalm.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V1">
    1
  </span>
  We have heard with our ears, God;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  our fathers have told us what work you did in their days,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in the days of old.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V2">
    2
  </span>
  You drove out the nations with your hand,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but you planted them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  You afflicted the peoples,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but you spread them abroad.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V3">
    3
  </span>
  For they didn’t get the land in possession by their own sword,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither did their own arm save them;
</div>
<div class="q">
  but your right hand, your arm, and the light of your face,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because you were favorable to them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V4">
    4
  </span>
  God, you are my King.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Command victories for Jacob!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V5">
    5
  </span>
  Through you, we will push down our adversaries.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Through your name, we will tread down those who rise up against us.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V6">
    6
  </span>
  For I will not trust in my bow,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither will my sword save me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V7">
    7
  </span>
  But you have saved us from our adversaries,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and have shamed those who hate us.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V8">
    8
  </span>
  In God we have made our boast all day long.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  We will give thanks to your name forever.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V9">
    9
  </span>
  But now you rejected us, and brought us to dishonor,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and don’t go out with our armies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V10">
    10
  </span>
  You make us turn back from the adversary.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Those who hate us take plunder for themselves.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V11">
    11
  </span>
  You have made us like sheep for food,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and have scattered us among the nations.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V12">
    12
  </span>
  You sell your people for nothing,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and have gained nothing from their sale.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V13">
    13
  </span>
  You make us a reproach to our neighbors,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a scoffing and a derision to those who are around us.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V14">
    14
  </span>
  You make us a byword among the nations,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a shaking of the head among the peoples.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V15">
    15
  </span>
  All day long my dishonor is before me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and shame covers my face,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V16">
    16
  </span>
  at the taunt of one who reproaches and verbally abuses,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because of the enemy and the avenger.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V17">
    17
  </span>
  All this has come on us,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  yet we haven’t forgotten you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  We haven’t been false to your covenant.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V18">
    18
  </span>
  Our heart has not turned back,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither have our steps strayed from your path,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V19">
    19
  </span>
  though you have crushed us in the haunt of jackals,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and covered us with the shadow of death.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V20">
    20
  </span>
  If we have forgotten the name of our God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  or spread out our hands to a strange god,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V21">
    21
  </span>
  won’t God search this out?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  For he knows the secrets of the heart.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V22">
    22
  </span>
  Yes, for your sake we are killed all day long.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  We are regarded as sheep for the slaughter.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V23">
    23
  </span>
  Wake up!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Why do you sleep, Lord?
  <a href="#PSA44FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      The word translated “Lord” is “Adonai.”
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q">
  Arise!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t reject us forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V24">
    24
  </span>
  Why do you hide your face,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and forget our affliction and our oppression?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V25">
    25
  </span>
  For our soul is bowed down to the dust.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Our body clings to the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA44V26">
    26
  </span>
  Rise up to help us.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Redeem us for your loving kindness’ sake.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
  <p class="f" id="PSA44FN1">
    <span class="notemark">
      †
    </span>
    <a class="notebackref" href="#PSA44V23">

    </a>

### 45

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. Set to “The Lilies.” A contemplation by the sons of Korah. A wedding song.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V1">
    1
  </span>
  My heart overflows with a noble theme.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I recite my verses for the king.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My tongue is like the pen of a skillful writer.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V2">
    2
  </span>
  You are the most excellent of the sons of men.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Grace has anointed your lips,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  therefore God has blessed you forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V3">
    3
  </span>
  Strap your sword on your thigh, O mighty one,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in your splendor and your majesty.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V4">
    4
  </span>
  In your majesty ride on victoriously on behalf of truth, humility, and righteousness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let your right hand display awesome deeds.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V5">
    5
  </span>
  Your arrows are sharp.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The nations fall under you, with arrows in the heart of the king’s enemies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V6">
    6
  </span>
  Your throne, God, is forever and ever.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  A scepter of equity is the scepter of your kingdom.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V7">
    7
  </span>
  You have loved righteousness, and hated wickedness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Therefore God, your God, has anointed you with the oil of gladness above your fellows.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V8">
    8
  </span>
  All your garments smell like myrrh, aloes, and cassia.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Out of ivory palaces stringed instruments have made you glad.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V9">
    9
  </span>
  Kings’ daughters are among your honorable women.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  At your right hand the queen stands in gold of Ophir.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V10">
    10
  </span>
  Listen, daughter, consider, and turn your ear.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Forget your own people, and also your father’s house.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V11">
    11
  </span>
  So the king will desire your beauty,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  honor him, for he is your lord.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V12">
    12
  </span>
  The daughter of Tyre comes with a gift.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The rich among the people entreat your favor.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V13">
    13
  </span>
  The princess inside is all glorious.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Her clothing is interwoven with gold.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V14">
    14
  </span>
  She shall be led to the king in embroidered work.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The virgins, her companions who follow her, shall be brought to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V15">
    15
  </span>
  With gladness and rejoicing they shall be led.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They shall enter into the king’s palace.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V16">
    16
  </span>
  Your sons will take the place of your fathers.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You shall make them princes in all the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA45V17">
    17
  </span>
  I will make your name to be remembered in all generations.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Therefore the peoples shall give you thanks forever and ever.

### 48

<div class="d">
  A Song. A Psalm by the sons of Korah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V1">
    1
  </span>
  Great is Yahweh, and greatly to be praised,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in the city of our God, in his holy mountain.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V2">
    2
  </span>
  Beautiful in elevation, the joy of the whole earth,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  is Mount Zion, on the north sides,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the city of the great King.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V3">
    3
  </span>
  God has shown himself in her citadels as a refuge.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V4">
    4
  </span>
  For, behold, the kings assembled themselves,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  they passed by together.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V5">
    5
  </span>
  They saw it, then they were amazed.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They were dismayed.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They hurried away.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V6">
    6
  </span>
  Trembling took hold of them there,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  pain, as of a woman in travail.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V7">
    7
  </span>
  With the east wind, you break the ships of Tarshish.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V8">
    8
  </span>
  As we have heard, so we have seen,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in the city of Yahweh of Armies, in the city of our God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  God will establish it forever.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V9">
    9
  </span>
  We have thought about your loving kindness, God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in the middle of your temple.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V10">
    10
  </span>
  As is your name, God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so is your praise to the ends of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your right hand is full of righteousness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V11">
    11
  </span>
  Let Mount Zion be glad!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the daughters of Judah rejoice because of your judgments.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V12">
    12
  </span>
  Walk about Zion, and go around her.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Number its towers.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V13">
    13
  </span>
  Notice her bulwarks.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Consider her palaces,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that you may tell it to the next generation.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA48V14">
    14
  </span>
  For this God is our God forever and ever.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He will be our guide even to death.
</div>

### 49

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by the sons of Korah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V1">
    1
  </span>
  Hear this, all you peoples.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Listen, all you inhabitants of the world,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V2">
    2
  </span>
  both low and high,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  rich and poor together.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V3">
    3
  </span>
  My mouth will speak words of wisdom.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My heart will utter understanding.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V4">
    4
  </span>
  I will incline my ear to a proverb.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will solve my riddle on the harp.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V5">
    5
  </span>
  Why should I fear in the days of evil,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  when iniquity at my heels surrounds me?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V6">
    6
  </span>
  Those who trust in their wealth,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and boast in the multitude of their riches—
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V7">
    7
  </span>
  none of them can by any means redeem his brother,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  nor give God a ransom for him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V8">
    8
  </span>
  For the redemption of their life is costly,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  no payment is ever enough,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V9">
    9
  </span>
  that he should live on forever,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that he should not see corruption.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V10">
    10
  </span>
  For he sees that wise men die;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  likewise the fool and the senseless perish,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and leave their wealth to others.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V11">
    11
  </span>
  Their inward thought is that their houses will endure forever,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and their dwelling places to all generations.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They name their lands after themselves.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V12">
    12
  </span>
  But man, despite his riches, doesn’t endure.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He is like the animals that perish.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V13">
    13
  </span>
  This is the destiny of those who are foolish,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and of those who approve their sayings.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V14">
    14
  </span>
  They are appointed as a flock for Sheol.
  <a href="#PSA49FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Death shall be their shepherd.
</div>
<div class="q">
  The upright shall have dominion over them in the morning.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Their beauty shall decay in Sheol,
  <a href="#PSA49FN2" class="notemark">
    ‡
    <span class="popup">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q2">
  far from their mansion.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V15">
    15
  </span>
  But God will redeem my soul from the power of Sheol,
  <a href="#PSA49FN3" class="notemark">
    §
    <span class="popup">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for he will receive me.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V16">
    16
  </span>
  Don’t be afraid when a man is made rich,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  when the glory of his house is increased;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V17">
    17
  </span>
  for when he dies he will carry nothing away.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His glory won’t descend after him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V18">
    18
  </span>
  Though while he lived he blessed his soul—
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and men praise you when you do well for yourself—
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V19">
    19
  </span>
  he shall go to the generation of his fathers.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They shall never see the light.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA49V20">
    20
  </span>
  A man who has riches without understanding,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  is like the animals that perish.
</div>

### 50

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V1">
    1
  </span>
  The Mighty One, God, Yahweh, speaks,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and calls the earth from sunrise to sunset.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V2">
    2
  </span>
  Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  God shines out.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V3">
    3
  </span>
  Our God comes, and does not keep silent.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  A fire devours before him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  It is very stormy around him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V4">
    4
  </span>
  He calls to the heavens above,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to the earth, that he may judge his people:
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V5">
    5
  </span>
  “Gather my saints together to me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  those who have made a covenant with me by sacrifice.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V6">
    6
  </span>
  The heavens shall declare his righteousness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for God himself is judge.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V7">
    7
  </span>
  “Hear, my people, and I will speak.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Israel, I will testify against you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  I am God, your God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V8">
    8
  </span>
  I don’t rebuke you for your sacrifices.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your burnt offerings are continually before me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V9">
    9
  </span>
  I have no need for a bull from your stall,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  nor male goats from your pens.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V10">
    10
  </span>
  For every animal of the forest is mine,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and the livestock on a thousand hills.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V11">
    11
  </span>
  I know all the birds of the mountains.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The wild animals of the field are mine.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V12">
    12
  </span>
  If I were hungry, I would not tell you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for the world is mine, and all that is in it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V13">
    13
  </span>
  Will I eat the meat of bulls,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  or drink the blood of goats?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V14">
    14
  </span>
  Offer to God the sacrifice of thanksgiving.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Pay your vows to the Most High.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V15">
    15
  </span>
  Call on me in the day of trouble.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will deliver you, and you will honor me.”
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V16">
    16
  </span>
  But to the wicked God says,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “What right do you have to declare my statutes,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that you have taken my covenant on your lips,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V17">
    17
  </span>
  since you hate instruction,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and throw my words behind you?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V18">
    18
  </span>
  When you saw a thief, you consented with him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and have participated with adulterers.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V19">
    19
  </span>
  “You give your mouth to evil.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your tongue frames deceit.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V20">
    20
  </span>
  You sit and speak against your brother.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You slander your own mother’s son.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V21">
    21
  </span>
  You have done these things, and I kept silent.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You thought that I was just like you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will rebuke you, and accuse you in front of your eyes.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V22">
    22
  </span>
  “Now consider this, you who forget God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  lest I tear you into pieces, and there be no one to deliver.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA50V23">
    23
  </span>
  Whoever offers the sacrifice of thanksgiving glorifies me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and prepares his way so that I will show God’s salvation to him.”
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 51

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David, when Nathan the prophet came to him, after he had gone in to Bathsheba.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V1">
    1
  </span>
  Have mercy on me, God, according to your loving kindness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  According to the multitude of your tender mercies, blot out my transgressions.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V2">
    2
  </span>
  Wash me thoroughly from my iniquity.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Cleanse me from my sin.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V3">
    3
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>

  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>

    6

</div>
<div class="q">

    7
  </span>

  </span>

</div>

  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V10">
    10
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>

  </span>

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V12">
    12
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V13">
    13
  </span>
  Then I will teach transgressors your ways.
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V14">
    14
  </span>
  Deliver me from the guilt of bloodshed, O God, the God of my salvation.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My tongue will sing aloud of your righteousness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V15">
    15
  </span>
  Lord, open my lips.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My mouth will declare your praise.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V16">
    16
  </span>
  For you don’t delight in sacrifice, or else I would give it.
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V17">
    17
  </span>

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA51V18">

  </span>

  </span>

### 52

<div class="d">

### 55

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A contemplation by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA55V1">
    1
  </span>
  Listen to my prayer, God.
</div>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA55V2">
    2
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA55V3">
    3
  </span>

</div>

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA55V4">
    4
  </span>

</div>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA55V5">
    5
  </span>

</div>

    6

  </span>
  For it was not an enemy who insulted me,
</div>

</div>

</div>

</div>

  </span>

  </span>

    </span>

  </span>

</div>

</div>

    17
  </span>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA55V18">

</div>

  </span>

### 56

<div class="d">

  <span class="verse" id="PSA56V10">

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA56V11">

  </span>
  I have put my trust in God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will not be afraid.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  What can man do to me?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA56V12">
    12
  </span>
  Your vows are on me, God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will give thank offerings to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA56V13">

  </span>

</div>

### 57

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A poem by David, when he fled from Saul, in the cave.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V1">
    1
  </span>
  Be merciful to me, God, be merciful to me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for my soul takes refuge in you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Yes, in the shadow of your wings, I will take refuge,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  until disaster has passed.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V2">
    2
  </span>
  I cry out to God Most High,
</div>
<div class="q">
  to God who accomplishes my requests for me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V3">
    3
  </span>
  He will send from heaven, and save me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  he rebukes the one who is pursuing me.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  God will send out his loving kindness and his truth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V4">
    4
  </span>
  My soul is among lions.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I lie among those who are set on fire,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  even the sons of men, whose teeth are spears and arrows,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and their tongue a sharp sword.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V5">
    5
  </span>
  Be exalted, God, above the heavens!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let your glory be above all the earth!
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V6">
    6
  </span>
  They have prepared a net for my steps.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My soul is bowed down.
</div>
<div class="q">
  They dig a pit before me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They fall into the middle of it themselves.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V7">
    7
  </span>
  My heart is steadfast, God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My heart is steadfast.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will sing, yes, I will sing praises.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V8">
    8
  </span>
  Wake up, my glory! Wake up, lute and harp!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will wake up the dawn.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V9">
    9
  </span>
  I will give thanks to you, Lord, among the peoples.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will sing praises to you among the nations.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V10">
    10
  </span>
  For your great loving kindness reaches to the heavens,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and your truth to the skies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA57V11">
    11
  </span>
  Be exalted, God, above the heavens.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let your glory be over all the earth.
</div>

  <hr/>
