### 58

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A poem by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V1">
    1
  </span>
  Do you indeed speak righteousness, silent ones?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Do you judge blamelessly, you sons of men?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V2">
    2
  </span>
  No, in your heart you plot injustice.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You measure out the violence of your hands in the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V3">
    3
  </span>
  The wicked go astray from the womb.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They are wayward as soon as they are born, speaking lies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V4">
    4
  </span>
  Their poison is like the poison of a snake,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  like a deaf cobra that stops its ear,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V5">
    5
  </span>
  which doesn’t listen to the voice of charmers,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  no matter how skillful the charmer may be.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V6">
    6
  </span>
  Break their teeth, God, in their mouth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Break out the great teeth of the young lions, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V7">
    7
  </span>
  Let them vanish like water that flows away.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  When they draw the bow, let their arrows be made blunt.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V8">
    8
  </span>
  Let them be like a snail which melts and passes away,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  like the stillborn child, who has not seen the sun.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V9">
    9
  </span>
  Before your pots can feel the heat of the thorns,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  he will sweep away the green and the burning alike.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V10">
    10
  </span>
  The righteous shall rejoice when he sees the vengeance.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He shall wash his feet in the blood of the wicked,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA58V11">
    11
  </span>
  so that men shall say, “Most certainly there is a reward for the righteous.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Most certainly there is a God who judges the earth.”
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 59

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A poem by David, when Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V1">
    1
  </span>
  Deliver me from my enemies, my God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Set me on high from those who rise up against me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V2">
    2
  </span>
  Deliver me from the workers of iniquity.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Save me from the bloodthirsty men.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V3">
    3
  </span>
  For, behold, they lie in wait for my soul.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The mighty gather themselves together against me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  not for my disobedience, nor for my sin, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V4">
    4
  </span>
  I have done no wrong, yet they are ready to attack me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Rise up, behold, and help me!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V5">
    5
  </span>
  You, Yahweh God of Armies, the God of Israel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  rouse yourself to punish the nations.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Show no mercy to the wicked traitors.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V6">
    6
  </span>
  They return at evening, howling like dogs,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and prowl around the city.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V7">
    7
  </span>
  Behold, they spew with their mouth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Swords are in their lips,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “For”, they say, “who hears us?”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V8">
    8
  </span>
  But you, Yahweh, laugh at them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You scoff at all the nations.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V9">
    9
  </span>
  Oh, my Strength, I watch for you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for God is my high tower.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V10">
    10
  </span>
  My God will go before me with his loving kindness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  God will let me look at my enemies in triumph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V11">
    11
  </span>
  Don’t kill them, or my people may forget.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Scatter them by your power, and bring them down, Lord our shield.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V12">
    12
  </span>
  For the sin of their mouth, and the words of their lips,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  let them be caught in their pride,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for the curses and lies which they utter.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V13">
    13
  </span>
  Consume them in wrath.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Consume them, and they will be no more.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Let them know that God rules in Jacob,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to the ends of the earth.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V14">
    14
  </span>
  At evening let them return.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let them howl like a dog, and go around the city.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V15">
    15
  </span>
  They shall wander up and down for food,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and wait all night if they aren’t satisfied.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V16">
    16
  </span>
  But I will sing of your strength.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yes, I will sing aloud of your loving kindness in the morning.
</div>
<div class="q">
  For you have been my high tower,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a refuge in the day of my distress.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA59V17">
    17
  </span>
  To you, my strength, I will sing praises.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  For God is my high tower, the God of my mercy.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 60

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “The Lily of the Covenant.” A teaching poem by David, when he fought with Aram Naharaim and with Aram Zobah, and Joab returned, and killed twelve thousand of Edom in the Valley of Salt.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V1">
    1
  </span>
  God, you have rejected us.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have broken us down.
</div>
<div class="q">
  You have been angry.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Restore us, again.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V2">
    2
  </span>
  You have made the land tremble.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have torn it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Mend its fractures,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for it quakes.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V3">
    3
  </span>
  You have shown your people hard things.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have made us drink the wine that makes us stagger.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V4">
    4
  </span>
  You have given a banner to those who fear you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that it may be displayed because of the truth.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V5">
    5
  </span>
  So that your beloved may be delivered,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  save with your right hand, and answer us.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V6">
    6
  </span>
  God has spoken from his sanctuary:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “I will triumph.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will divide Shechem,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and measure out the valley of Succoth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V7">
    7
  </span>
  Gilead is mine, and Manasseh is mine.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Ephraim also is the defense of my head.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Judah is my scepter.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V8">
    8
  </span>
  Moab is my wash basin.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will throw my sandal on Edom.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I shout in triumph over Philistia.”
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V9">
    9
  </span>
  Who will bring me into the strong city?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Who has led me to Edom?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V10">
    10
  </span>
  Haven’t you, God, rejected us?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You don’t go out with our armies, God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V11">
    11
  </span>
  Give us help against the adversary,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for the help of man is vain.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA60V12">
    12
  </span>
  Through God we will do valiantly,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for it is he who will tread down our adversaries.
</div>

  <hr/>

### 61

<div class="d">

    2
  </span>

</div>

  Lead me to the rock that is higher than I.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA61V3">
    3
  </span>
  For you have been a refuge for me,
</div>
<div class="q2">

  <span class="verse" id="PSA61V4">
    4
  </span>

<div class="q2">

<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA61V5">
    5
  </span>

### 62

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. To Jeduthun. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V1">
    1
  </span>
  My soul rests in God alone.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My salvation is from him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V2">
    2
  </span>
  He alone is my rock, my salvation, and my fortress.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will never be greatly shaken.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V3">
    3
  </span>
  How long will you assault a man?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Would all of you throw him down,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  like a leaning wall, like a tottering fence?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V4">
    4
  </span>
  They fully intend to throw him down from his lofty place.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They delight in lies.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They bless with their mouth, but they curse inwardly.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V5">
    5
  </span>
  My soul, wait in silence for God alone,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for my expectation is from him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V6">
    6
  </span>
  He alone is my rock and my salvation, my fortress.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will not be shaken.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V7">
    7
  </span>
  My salvation and my honor is with God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The rock of my strength, and my refuge, is in God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V8">
    8
  </span>
  Trust in him at all times, you people.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Pour out your heart before him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  God is a refuge for us.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V9">
    9
  </span>
  Surely men of low degree are just a breath,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and men of high degree are a lie.
</div>
<div class="q">
  In the balances they will go up.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They are together lighter than a breath.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V10">
    10
  </span>
  Don’t trust in oppression.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t become vain in robbery.
</div>
<div class="q">
  If riches increase,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  don’t set your heart on them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V11">
    11
  </span>
  God has spoken once;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  twice I have heard this,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that power belongs to God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA62V12">
    12
  </span>
  Also to you, Lord, belongs loving kindness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you reward every man according to his work.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 63

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by David, when he was in the desert of Judah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V1">
    1
  </span>
  God, you are my God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will earnestly seek you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  My soul thirsts for you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My flesh longs for you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in a dry and weary land, where there is no water.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V2">
    2
  </span>
  So I have seen you in the sanctuary,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  watching your power and your glory.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V3">
    3
  </span>
  Because your loving kindness is better than life,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my lips shall praise you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V4">
    4
  </span>
  So I will bless you while I live.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will lift up my hands in your name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V5">
    5
  </span>
  My soul shall be satisfied as with the richest food.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My mouth shall praise you with joyful lips,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V6">
    6
  </span>
  when I remember you on my bed,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and think about you in the night watches.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V7">
    7
  </span>
  For you have been my help.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will rejoice in the shadow of your wings.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V8">
    8
  </span>
  My soul stays close to you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your right hand holds me up.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V9">
    9
  </span>
  But those who seek my soul to destroy it
</div>
<div class="q2">
  shall go into the lower parts of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V10">
    10
  </span>
  They shall be given over to the power of the sword.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They shall be jackal food.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA63V11">
    11
  </span>
  But the king shall rejoice in God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Everyone who swears by him will praise him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for the mouth of those who speak lies shall be silenced.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 64

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V1">
    1
  </span>
  Hear my voice, God, in my complaint.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Preserve my life from fear of the enemy.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V2">
    2
  </span>
  Hide me from the conspiracy of the wicked,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  from the noisy crowd of the ones doing evil;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V3">
    3
  </span>
  who sharpen their tongue like a sword,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and aim their arrows, deadly words,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V4">
    4
  </span>
  to shoot innocent men from ambushes.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They shoot at him suddenly and fearlessly.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V5">
    5
  </span>
  They encourage themselves in evil plans.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They talk about laying snares secretly.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They say, “Who will see them?”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V6">
    6
  </span>
  They plot injustice, saying, “We have made a perfect plan!”
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Surely man’s mind and heart are cunning.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V7">
    7
  </span>
  But God will shoot at them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They will be suddenly struck down with an arrow.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V8">
    8
  </span>
  Their own tongues shall ruin them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All who see them will shake their heads.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V9">
    9
  </span>
  All mankind shall be afraid.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They shall declare the work of God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and shall wisely ponder what he has done.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA64V10">
    10
  </span>
  The righteous shall be glad in Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and shall take refuge in him.
</div>
<div class="q2">

### 68

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. A song.

<div class="q">

    1
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>

<div class="q">

    2
  </span>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA68V3">
    3
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA68V4">
    4
  </span>

</div>

</div>

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA68V10">

  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">

</div>

<div class="q">

  </span>

</div>

### 69

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Lilies.” By David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V1">
    1
  </span>
  Save me, God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for the waters have come up to my neck!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V2">
    2
  </span>
  I sink in deep mire, where there is no foothold.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have come into deep waters, where the floods overflow me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V3">
    3
  </span>
  I am weary with my crying.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My throat is dry.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My eyes fail looking for my God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V4">
    4
  </span>
  Those who hate me without a cause are more than the hairs of my head.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Those who want to cut me off, being my enemies wrongfully, are mighty.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have to restore what I didn’t take away.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V5">
    5
  </span>
  God, you know my foolishness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My sins aren’t hidden from you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V6">
    6
  </span>
  Don’t let those who wait for you be shamed through me, Lord Yahweh of Armies.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t let those who seek you be brought to dishonor through me, God of Israel.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V7">
    7
  </span>
  Because for your sake, I have borne reproach.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Shame has covered my face.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V8">
    8
  </span>
  I have become a stranger to my brothers,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  an alien to my mother’s children.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V9">
    9
  </span>
  For the zeal of your house consumes me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The reproaches of those who reproach you have fallen on me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V10">
    10
  </span>
  When I wept and I fasted,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that was to my reproach.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V11">
    11
  </span>
  When I made sackcloth my clothing,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I became a byword to them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V12">
    12
  </span>
  Those who sit in the gate talk about me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I am the song of the drunkards.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V13">
    13
  </span>
  But as for me, my prayer is to you, Yahweh, in an acceptable time.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  God, in the abundance of your loving kindness, answer me in the truth of your salvation.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V14">
    14
  </span>
  Deliver me out of the mire, and don’t let me sink.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let me be delivered from those who hate me, and out of the deep waters.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V15">
    15
  </span>
  Don’t let the flood waters overwhelm me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither let the deep swallow me up.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t let the pit shut its mouth on me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V16">
    16
  </span>
  Answer me, Yahweh, for your loving kindness is good.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  According to the multitude of your tender mercies, turn to me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V17">
    17
  </span>
  Don’t hide your face from your servant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I am in distress.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Answer me speedily!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V18">
    18
  </span>
  Draw near to my soul and redeem it.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Ransom me because of my enemies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V19">
    19
  </span>
  You know my reproach, my shame, and my dishonor.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My adversaries are all before you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V20">
    20
  </span>
  Reproach has broken my heart, and I am full of heaviness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I looked for some to take pity, but there was none;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for comforters, but I found none.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V21">
    21
  </span>
  They also gave me poison for my food.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In my thirst, they gave me vinegar to drink.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V22">
    22
  </span>
  Let their table before them become a snare.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  May it become a retribution and a trap.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V23">
    23
  </span>
  Let their eyes be darkened, so that they can’t see.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let their backs be continually bent.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V24">
    24
  </span>
  Pour out your indignation on them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the fierceness of your anger overtake them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V25">
    25
  </span>
  Let their habitation be desolate.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let no one dwell in their tents.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V26">
    26
  </span>
  For they persecute him whom you have wounded.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They tell of the sorrow of those whom you have hurt.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V27">
    27
  </span>
  Charge them with crime upon crime.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t let them come into your righteousness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V28">
    28
  </span>
  Let them be blotted out of the book of life,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and not be written with the righteous.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V29">
    29
  </span>
  But I am in pain and distress.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let your salvation, God, protect me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V30">
    30
  </span>
  I will praise the name of God with a song,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and will magnify him with thanksgiving.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V31">
    31
  </span>
  It will please Yahweh better than an ox,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  or a bull that has horns and hoofs.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V32">
    32
  </span>
  The humble have seen it, and are glad.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You who seek after God, let your heart live.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V33">
    33
  </span>
  For Yahweh hears the needy,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and doesn’t despise his captive people.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V34">
    34
  </span>
  Let heaven and earth praise him;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the seas, and everything that moves therein!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V35">
    35
  </span>
  For God will save Zion, and build the cities of Judah.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They shall settle there, and own it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA69V36">
    36
  </span>
  The children also of his servants shall inherit it.
</div>
<div class="q2">

### 70

<div class="d">

    1
  </span>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA70V2">
    2
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA70V3">
    3
  </span>

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA70V4">
    4

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA70V5">

</div>

### 71

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V1">
    1
  </span>
  In you, Yahweh, I take refuge.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Never let me be disappointed.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V2">
    2
  </span>
  Deliver me in your righteousness, and rescue me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Turn your ear to me, and save me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V3">
    3
  </span>
  Be to me a rock of refuge to which I may always go.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Give the command to save me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you are my rock and my fortress.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V4">
    4
  </span>
  Rescue me, my God, from the hand of the wicked,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  from the hand of the unrighteous and cruel man.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V5">
    5
  </span>
  For you are my hope, Lord Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my confidence from my youth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V6">
    6
  </span>
  I have relied on you from the womb.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You are he who took me out of my mother’s womb.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will always praise you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V7">
    7
  </span>
  I am a marvel to many,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but you are my strong refuge.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V8">
    8
  </span>
  My mouth shall be filled with your praise,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  with your honor all day long.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V9">
    9
  </span>
  Don’t reject me in my old age.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t forsake me when my strength fails.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V10">
    10
  </span>
  For my enemies talk about me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Those who watch for my soul conspire together,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V11">
    11
  </span>
  saying, “God has forsaken him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Pursue and take him, for no one will rescue him.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V12">
    12
  </span>
  God, don’t be far from me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My God, hurry to help me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V13">
    13
  </span>
  Let my accusers be disappointed and consumed.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let them be covered with disgrace and scorn who want to harm me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V14">
    14
  </span>
  But I will always hope,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and will add to all of your praise.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V15">
    15
  </span>
  My mouth will tell about your righteousness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and of your salvation all day,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  though I don’t know its full measure.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V16">
    16
  </span>
  I will come with the mighty acts of the Lord Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will make mention of your righteousness, even of yours alone.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V17">
    17
  </span>
  God, you have taught me from my youth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Until now, I have declared your wondrous works.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V18">
    18
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  until I have declared your strength to the next generation,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  your might to everyone who is to come.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V19">
    19
  </span>
  God, your righteousness also reaches to the heavens.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have done great things.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  God, who is like you?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V20">

  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  you will let me live.
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V21">
    21
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  and comfort me again.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V22">
    22
  </span>
  I will also praise you with the harp for your faithfulness, my God.
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V23">
    23
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  My soul, which you have redeemed, sings praises to you!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA71V24">
    24
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  for they are disappointed, and they are confounded,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who want to harm me.

### 72

<div class="d">
  By Solomon.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V1">
    1
  </span>
  God, give the king your justice;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  your righteousness to the royal son.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V2">
    2
  </span>
  He will judge your people with righteousness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and your poor with justice.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V3">
    3
  </span>
  The mountains shall bring prosperity to the people.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The hills bring the fruit of righteousness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V4">
    4
  </span>
  He will judge the poor of the people.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He will save the children of the needy,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and will break the oppressor in pieces.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V5">
    5
  </span>
  They shall fear you while the sun endures;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and as long as the moon, throughout all generations.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V6">
    6
  </span>
  He will come down like rain on the mown grass,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  as showers that water the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V7">
    7
  </span>
  In his days, the righteous shall flourish,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and abundance of peace, until the moon is no more.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V8">
    8
  </span>
  He shall have dominion also from sea to sea,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  from the River to the ends of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V9">
    9
  </span>
  Those who dwell in the wilderness shall bow before him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His enemies shall lick the dust.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V10">
    10
  </span>
  The kings of Tarshish and of the islands will bring tribute.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V11">
    11
  </span>
  Yes, all kings shall fall down before him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All nations shall serve him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V12">
    12
  </span>
  For he will deliver the needy when he cries;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the poor, who has no helper.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V13">
    13
  </span>
  He will have pity on the poor and needy.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He will save the souls of the needy.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V14">
    14
  </span>
  He will redeem their soul from oppression and violence.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Their blood will be precious in his sight.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V15">
    15
  </span>
  He will live; and Sheba’s gold will be given to him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Men will pray for him continually.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They will bless him all day long.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V16">
    16
  </span>
  Abundance of grain shall be throughout the land.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Its fruit sways like Lebanon.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let it flourish, thriving like the grass of the field.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V17">
    17
  </span>
  His name endures forever.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His name continues as long as the sun.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Men shall be blessed by him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All nations will call him blessed.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V18">
    18
  </span>
  Praise be to Yahweh God, the God of Israel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who alone does marvelous deeds.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA72V19">
    19
  </span>
  Blessed be his glorious name forever!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the whole earth be filled with his glory!
</div>
<div class="q">
  Amen and amen.
</div>
<div class="b">

### 73

<div class="ms">
  BOOK 3
</div>
<div class="d">
  A Psalm by Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V1">
    1
  </span>
  Surely God
  <a href="#PSA73FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      The Hebrew word rendered “God” is “אֱלֹהִ֑ים” (Elohim).
    </span>
  </a>
  is good to Israel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to those who are pure in heart.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V2">
    2
  </span>
  But as for me, my feet were almost gone.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My steps had nearly slipped.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V3">
    3
  </span>
  For I was envious of the arrogant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  when I saw the prosperity of the wicked.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V4">
    4
  </span>
  For there are no struggles in their death,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but their strength is firm.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V5">
    5
  </span>
  They are free from burdens of men,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither are they plagued like other men.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V6">
    6
  </span>
  Therefore pride is like a chain around their neck.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Violence covers them like a garment.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V7">
    7
  </span>
  Their eyes bulge with fat.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Their minds pass the limits of conceit.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V8">
    8
  </span>
  They scoff and speak with malice.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In arrogance, they threaten oppression.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V9">
    9
  </span>
  They have set their mouth in the heavens.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Their tongue walks through the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V10">
    10
  </span>
  Therefore their people return to them,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and they drink up waters of abundance.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V11">
    11
  </span>
  They say, “How does God know?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Is there knowledge in the Most High?”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V12">
    12
  </span>
  Behold, these are the wicked.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Being always at ease, they increase in riches.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V13">
    13
  </span>
  Surely I have cleansed my heart in vain,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and washed my hands in innocence,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V14">
    14
  </span>
  For all day long I have been plagued,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and punished every morning.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V15">
    15
  </span>
  If I had said, “I will speak thus”,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  behold, I would have betrayed the generation of your children.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V16">
    16
  </span>
  When I tried to understand this,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  it was too painful for me—
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V17">
    17
  </span>
  until I entered God’s sanctuary,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and considered their latter end.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V18">
    18
  </span>
  Surely you set them in slippery places.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You throw them down to destruction.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V19">
    19
  </span>
  How they are suddenly destroyed!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They are completely swept away with terrors.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V20">
    20
  </span>
  As a dream when one wakes up,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so, Lord,
  <a href="#PSA73FN2" class="notemark">
    ‡
    <span class="popup">
      The word translated “Lord” is “Adonai.”
    </span>
  </a>
  when you awake, you will despise their fantasies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V21">
    21
  </span>
  For my soul was grieved.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I was embittered in my heart.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V22">
    22
  </span>
  I was so senseless and ignorant.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I was a brute beast before you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V23">
    23
  </span>
  Nevertheless, I am continually with you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have held my right hand.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V24">
    24
  </span>
  You will guide me with your counsel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and afterward receive me to glory.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V25">
    25
  </span>
  Whom do I have in heaven?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  There is no one on earth whom I desire besides you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V26">
    26
  </span>
  My flesh and my heart fails,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but God is the strength of my heart and my portion forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V27">
    27
  </span>
  For, behold, those who are far from you shall perish.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have destroyed all those who are unfaithful to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA73V28">
    28
  </span>
  But it is good for me to come close to God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have made the Lord Yahweh
  <a href="#PSA73FN3" class="notemark">
    §
    <span class="popup">
      “Yahweh” is God’s proper Name, sometimes rendered “LORD” (all caps) in other translations.
    </span>
  </a>
  my refuge,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that I may tell of all your works.

### 74

<div class="d">
  A contemplation by Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V1">
    1
  </span>
  God, why have you rejected us forever?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Why does your anger smolder against the sheep of your pasture?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V2">
    2
  </span>
  Remember your congregation, which you purchased of old,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  which you have redeemed to be the tribe of your inheritance:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Mount Zion, in which you have lived.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V3">
    3
  </span>
  Lift up your feet to the perpetual ruins,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  all the evil that the enemy has done in the sanctuary.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V4">
    4
  </span>
  Your adversaries have roared in the middle of your assembly.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They have set up their standards as signs.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V5">
    5
  </span>
  They behaved like men wielding axes,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  cutting through a thicket of trees.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V6">
    6
  </span>
  Now they break all its carved work down with hatchet and hammers.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V7">
    7
  </span>
  They have burned your sanctuary to the ground.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They have profaned the dwelling place of your Name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V8">
    8
  </span>
  They said in their heart, “We will crush them completely.”
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They have burned up all the places in the land where God was worshiped.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V9">
    9
  </span>
  We see no miraculous signs.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  There is no longer any prophet,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither is there among us anyone who knows how long.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V10">
    10
  </span>
  How long, God, shall the adversary reproach?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Shall the enemy blaspheme your name forever?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V11">
    11
  </span>
  Why do you draw back your hand, even your right hand?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Take it from your chest and consume them!
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V12">
    12
  </span>
  Yet God is my King of old,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  working salvation throughout the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V13">
    13
  </span>
  You divided the sea by your strength.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You broke the heads of the sea monsters in the waters.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V14">
    14
  </span>
  You broke the heads of Leviathan in pieces.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You gave him as food to people and desert creatures.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V15">
    15
  </span>
  You opened up spring and stream.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You dried up mighty rivers.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V16">
    16
  </span>
  The day is yours, the night is also yours.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have prepared the light and the sun.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V17">
    17
  </span>
  You have set all the boundaries of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have made summer and winter.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V18">
    18
  </span>
  Remember this, that the enemy has mocked you, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Foolish people have blasphemed your name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V19">
    19
  </span>
  Don’t deliver the soul of your dove to wild beasts.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t forget the life of your poor forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V20">
    20
  </span>
  Honor your covenant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for haunts of violence fill the dark places of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V21">
    21
  </span>
  Don’t let the oppressed return ashamed.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the poor and needy praise your name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V22">
    22
  </span>
  Arise, God! Plead your own cause.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Remember how the foolish man mocks you all day.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA74V23">
    23
  </span>
  Don’t forget the voice of your adversaries.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The tumult of those who rise up against you ascends continually.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>

  <hr/>

### 75

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A Psalm by Asaph. A song.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V1">
    1
  </span>
  We give thanks to you, God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  We give thanks, for your Name is near.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Men tell about your wondrous works.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V2">
    2
  </span>
  When I choose the appointed time,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will judge blamelessly.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V3">
    3
  </span>
  The earth and all its inhabitants quake.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I firmly hold its pillars.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V4">
    4
  </span>
  I said to the arrogant, “Don’t boast!”
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I said to the wicked, “Don’t lift up the horn.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V5">
    5
  </span>
  Don’t lift up your horn on high.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t speak with a stiff neck.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V6">
    6
  </span>
  For neither from the east, nor from the west,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  nor yet from the south, comes exaltation.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V7">
    7
  </span>
  But God is the judge.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He puts down one, and lifts up another.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V8">
    8
  </span>
  For in Yahweh’s hand there is a cup,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  full of foaming wine mixed with spices.
</div>
<div class="q">
  He pours it out.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Indeed the wicked of the earth drink and drink it to its very dregs.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V9">
    9
  </span>
  But I will declare this forever:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will sing praises to the God of Jacob.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA75V10">
    10
  </span>
  I will cut off all the horns of the wicked,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but the horns of the righteous shall be lifted up.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>

### 76

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A Psalm by Asaph. A song.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V1">
    1
  </span>
  In Judah, God is known.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His name is great in Israel.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V2">
    2
  </span>
  His tabernacle is also in Salem.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His dwelling place in Zion.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V3">
    3
  </span>
  There he broke the flaming arrows of the bow,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the shield, and the sword, and the weapons of war.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V4">
    4
  </span>
  Glorious are you, and excellent,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  more than mountains of game.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V5">
    5
  </span>
  Valiant men lie plundered,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  they have slept their last sleep.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  None of the men of war can lift their hands.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V6">
    6
  </span>
  At your rebuke, God of Jacob,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  both chariot and horse are cast into a dead sleep.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V7">
    7
  </span>
  You, even you, are to be feared.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Who can stand in your sight when you are angry?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V8">
    8
  </span>
  You pronounced judgment from heaven.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The earth feared, and was silent,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V9">
    9
  </span>
  when God arose to judgment,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to save all the afflicted ones of the earth.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V10">
    10
  </span>
  Surely the wrath of man praises you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The survivors of your wrath are restrained.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V11">
    11
  </span>
  Make vows to Yahweh your God, and fulfill them!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let all of his neighbors bring presents to him who is to be feared.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA76V12">
    12
  </span>
  He will cut off the spirit of princes.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He is feared by the kings of the earth.
</div>
<div class="b">

### 77

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. To Jeduthun. A Psalm by Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V1">
    1
  </span>
  My cry goes to God!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Indeed, I cry to God for help,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and for him to listen to me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V2">
    2
  </span>
  In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My hand was stretched out in the night, and didn’t get tired.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My soul refused to be comforted.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V3">
    3
  </span>
  I remember God, and I groan.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I complain, and my spirit is overwhelmed.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V4">
    4
  </span>
  You hold my eyelids open.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I am so troubled that I can’t speak.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V5">
    5
  </span>
  I have considered the days of old,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the years of ancient times.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V6">
    6
  </span>
  I remember my song in the night.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I consider in my own heart;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my spirit diligently inquires:
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V7">
    7
  </span>
  “Will the Lord reject us forever?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Will he be favorable no more?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V8">
    8
  </span>
  Has his loving kindness vanished forever?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Does his promise fail for generations?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V9">
    9
  </span>
  Has God forgotten to be gracious?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Has he, in anger, withheld his compassion?”
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V10">
    10
  </span>
  Then I thought, “I will appeal to this:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the years of the right hand of the Most High.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V11">
    11
  </span>
  I will remember Yah’s deeds;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I will remember your wonders of old.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V12">
    12
  </span>
  I will also meditate on all your work,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and consider your doings.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V13">
    13
  </span>
  Your way, God, is in the sanctuary.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  What god is great like God?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V14">
    14
  </span>
  You are the God who does wonders.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have made your strength known among the peoples.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V15">
    15
  </span>
  You have redeemed your people with your arm,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the sons of Jacob and Joseph.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V16">
    16
  </span>
  The waters saw you, God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The waters saw you, and they writhed.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The depths also convulsed.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V17">
    17
  </span>
  The clouds poured out water.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The skies resounded with thunder.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your arrows also flashed around.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V18">
    18
  </span>
  The voice of your thunder was in the whirlwind.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The lightnings lit up the world.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The earth trembled and shook.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V19">
    19
  </span>
  Your way was through the sea,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  your paths through the great waters.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your footsteps were not known.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA77V20">
    20
  </span>
  You led your people like a flock,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  by the hand of Moses and Aaron.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>

  <hr/>

### 78

<div class="d">
  A contemplation by Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V1">
    1
  </span>
  Hear my teaching, my people.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Turn your ears to the words of my mouth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V2">
    2
  </span>
  I will open my mouth in a parable.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will utter dark sayings of old,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V3">
    3
  </span>
  which we have heard and known,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and our fathers have told us.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V4">
    4
  </span>
  We will not hide them from their children,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  telling to the generation to come the praises of Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  his strength, and his wondrous deeds that he has done.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V5">
    5
  </span>
  For he established a covenant in Jacob,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and appointed a teaching in Israel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  which he commanded our fathers,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that they should make them known to their children;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V6">
    6
  </span>
  that the generation to come might know, even the children who should be born;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who should arise and tell their children,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V7">
    7
  </span>
  that they might set their hope in God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and not forget God’s deeds,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but keep his commandments,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V8">
    8
  </span>
  and might not be as their fathers—
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a stubborn and rebellious generation,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a generation that didn’t make their hearts loyal,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  whose spirit was not steadfast with God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V9">
    9
  </span>
  The children of Ephraim, being armed and carrying bows,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  turned back in the day of battle.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V10">
    10
  </span>
  They didn’t keep God’s covenant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and refused to walk in his law.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V11">
    11
  </span>
  They forgot his doings,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  his wondrous deeds that he had shown them.

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V14">
    14
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  and all night with a light of fire.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V15">
    15
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  and gave them drink abundantly as out of the depths.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V16">
    16
  </span>
  He brought streams also out of the rock,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and caused waters to run down like rivers.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V17">
    17
  </span>

</div>

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V18">
    18
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V19">
    19
  </span>

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V20">

  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  and streams overflowed.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Can he give bread also?
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V21">
    21
  </span>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V23">

  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V24">
    24

</div>
<div class="q2">

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V25">

  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V26">

<div class="q">

  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V35">

  </span>

    54
  </span>

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V55">

  </span>

</div>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V56">
    56
  </span>
  Yet they tempted and rebelled against the Most High God,
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V57">
    57
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  They were twisted like a deceitful bow.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V58">
    58
  </span>
  For they provoked him to anger with their high places,
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V59">
    59
  </span>
  When God heard this, he was angry,
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V61">
    61
  </span>
  and delivered his strength into captivity,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  his glory into the adversary’s hand.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V62">
    62
  </span>
  He also gave his people over to the sword,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and was angry with his inheritance.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V63">
    63
  </span>
  Fire devoured their young men.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Their virgins had no wedding song.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V64">
    64
  </span>
  Their priests fell by the sword,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and their widows couldn’t weep.
</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V65">
    65
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V66">
    66
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V67">
    67
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  and didn’t choose the tribe of Ephraim,

  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V68">
    68
  </span>

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V69">
    69
  </span>
  He built his sanctuary like the heights,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  like the earth which he has established forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V70">
    70
  </span>
  He also chose David his servant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and took him from the sheepfolds;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V71">
    71
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  he brought him to be the shepherd of Jacob, his people,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and Israel, his inheritance.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA78V72">
    72
  </span>
  So he was their shepherd according to the integrity of his heart,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and guided them by the skillfulness of his hands.

### 79

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V1">
    1
  </span>
  God, the nations have come into your inheritance.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They have defiled your holy temple.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They have laid Jerusalem in heaps.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V2">
    2
  </span>
  They have given the dead bodies of your servants to be food for the birds of the sky,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the flesh of your saints to the animals of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V3">
    3
  </span>
  They have shed their blood like water around Jerusalem.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  There was no one to bury them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V4">
    4
  </span>
  We have become a reproach to our neighbors,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  a scoffing and derision to those who are around us.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V5">
    5
  </span>
  How long, Yahweh?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Will you be angry forever?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Will your jealousy burn like fire?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V6">
    6
  </span>
  Pour out your wrath on the nations that don’t know you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  on the kingdoms that don’t call on your name,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V7">
    7
  </span>
  for they have devoured Jacob,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and destroyed his homeland.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V8">
    8
  </span>
  Don’t hold the iniquities of our forefathers against us.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let your tender mercies speedily meet us,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for we are in desperate need.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V9">
    9
  </span>
  Help us, God of our salvation, for the glory of your name.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Deliver us, and forgive our sins, for your name’s sake.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V10">
    10
  </span>
  Why should the nations say, “Where is their God?”
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let it be known among the nations, before our eyes,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that vengeance for your servants’ blood is being poured out.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V11">
    11
  </span>
  Let the sighing of the prisoner come before you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  According to the greatness of your power, preserve those who are sentenced to death.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V12">
    12
  </span>
  Pay back to our neighbors seven times into their bosom
</div>
<div class="q2">
  their reproach with which they have reproached you, Lord.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA79V13">
    13
  </span>
  So we, your people and sheep of your pasture,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  will give you thanks forever.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  We will praise you forever, to all generations.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 80

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “The Lilies of the Covenant.” A Psalm by Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V1">
    1
  </span>
  Hear us, Shepherd of Israel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  you who lead Joseph like a flock,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  you who sit above the cherubim, shine out.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V2">
    2
  </span>
  Before Ephraim, Benjamin, and Manasseh, stir up your might!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Come to save us!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V3">
    3
  </span>
  Turn us again, God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Cause your face to shine,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and we will be saved.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V4">
    4
  </span>
  Yahweh God of Armies,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  how long will you be angry against the prayer of your people?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V5">
    5
  </span>
  You have fed them with the bread of tears,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and given them tears to drink in large measure.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V6">
    6
  </span>
  You make us a source of contention to our neighbors.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Our enemies laugh among themselves.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V7">
    7
  </span>
  Turn us again, God of Armies.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Cause your face to shine,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and we will be saved.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V8">
    8
  </span>
  You brought a vine out of Egypt.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You drove out the nations, and planted it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V9">
    9
  </span>
  You cleared the ground for it.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  It took deep root, and filled the land.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V10">
    10
  </span>
  The mountains were covered with its shadow.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Its boughs were like God’s cedars.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V11">
    11
  </span>
  It sent out its branches to the sea,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  its shoots to the River.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V12">
    12
  </span>
  Why have you broken down its walls,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so that all those who pass by the way pluck it?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V13">
    13
  </span>
  The boar out of the wood ravages it.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The wild animals of the field feed on it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V14">
    14
  </span>
  Turn again, we beg you, God of Armies.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Look down from heaven, and see, and visit this vine,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V15">
    15
  </span>
  the stock which your right hand planted,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the branch that you made strong for yourself.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V16">
    16
  </span>
  It’s burned with fire.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  It’s cut down.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They perish at your rebuke.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V17">
    17
  </span>
  Let your hand be on the man of your right hand,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  on the son of man whom you made strong for yourself.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V18">
    18
  </span>
  So we will not turn away from you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Revive us, and we will call on your name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA80V19">
    19
  </span>
  Turn us again, Yahweh God of Armies.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Cause your face to shine, and we will be saved.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 81

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. On an instrument of Gath. By Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V1">
    1
  </span>
  Sing aloud to God, our strength!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Make a joyful shout to the God of Jacob!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V2">
    2
  </span>
  Raise a song, and bring here the tambourine,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the pleasant lyre with the harp.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V3">
    3
  </span>
  Blow the trumpet at the New Moon,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  at the full moon, on our feast day.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V4">
    4
  </span>
  For it is a statute for Israel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  an ordinance of the God of Jacob.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V5">
    5
  </span>
  He appointed it in Joseph for a covenant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  when he went out over the land of Egypt,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I heard a language that I didn’t know.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V6">
    6
  </span>
  “I removed his shoulder from the burden.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His hands were freed from the basket.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V7">
    7
  </span>
  You called in trouble, and I delivered you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I answered you in the secret place of thunder.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I tested you at the waters of Meribah.”
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V8">
    8
  </span>
  “Hear, my people, and I will testify to you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Israel, if you would listen to me!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V9">
    9
  </span>
  There shall be no strange god in you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither shall you worship any foreign god.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V10">
    10
  </span>
  I am Yahweh, your God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who brought you up out of the land of Egypt.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Open your mouth wide, and I will fill it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V11">
    11
  </span>
  But my people didn’t listen to my voice.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Israel desired none of me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V12">
    12
  </span>
  So I let them go after the stubbornness of their hearts,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that they might walk in their own counsels.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V13">
    13
  </span>
  Oh that my people would listen to me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that Israel would walk in my ways!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V14">
    14
  </span>
  I would soon subdue their enemies,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and turn my hand against their adversaries.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V15">
    15
  </span>
  The haters of Yahweh would cringe before him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and their punishment would last forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA81V16">
    16
  </span>
  But he would have also fed them with the finest of the wheat.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will satisfy you with honey out of the rock.”
</div>

### 82

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA82V1">
    1
  </span>
  God presides in the great assembly.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He judges among the gods.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA82V2">
    2
  </span>
  “How long will you judge unjustly,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and show partiality to the wicked?”
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA82V3">
    3
  </span>
  “Defend the weak, the poor, and the fatherless.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Maintain the rights of the poor and oppressed.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA82V4">
    4
  </span>
  Rescue the weak and needy.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Deliver them out of the hand of the wicked.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA82V5">
    5
  </span>
  They don’t know, neither do they understand.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They walk back and forth in darkness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All the foundations of the earth are shaken.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA82V6">
    6
  </span>
  I said, “You are gods,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  all of you are sons of the Most High.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA82V7">
    7
  </span>
  Nevertheless you shall die like men,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and fall like one of the rulers.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA82V8">
    8
  </span>
  Arise, God, judge the earth,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you inherit all of the nations.
</div>

### 83

<div class="d">
  A song. A Psalm by Asaph.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V1">
    1
  </span>
  God, don’t keep silent.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t keep silent,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and don’t be still, God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V2">
    2
  </span>
  For, behold, your enemies are stirred up.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Those who hate you have lifted up their heads.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V3">
    3
  </span>
  They conspire with cunning against your people.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They plot against your cherished ones.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V4">
    4
  </span>
  “Come,” they say, “let’s destroy them as a nation,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that the name of Israel may be remembered no more.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V5">
    5
  </span>
  For they have conspired together with one mind.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They form an alliance against you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V6">
    6
  </span>
  The tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Moab, and the Hagrites;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V7">
    7
  </span>
  Gebal, Ammon, and Amalek;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Philistia with the inhabitants of Tyre;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V8">
    8
  </span>
  Assyria also is joined with them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They have helped the children of Lot.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V9">
    9
  </span>
  Do to them as you did to Midian,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  as to Sisera, as to Jabin, at the river Kishon;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V10">
    10
  </span>
  who perished at Endor,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who became as dung for the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V11">
    11
  </span>
  Make their nobles like Oreb and Zeeb,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  yes, all their princes like Zebah and Zalmunna,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V12">
    12
  </span>
  who said, “Let’s take possession of God’s pasture lands.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V13">
    13
  </span>
  My God, make them like tumbleweed,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  like chaff before the wind.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V14">
    14
  </span>
  As the fire that burns the forest,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  as the flame that sets the mountains on fire,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V15">
    15
  </span>
  so pursue them with your tempest,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and terrify them with your storm.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V16">
    16
  </span>
  Fill their faces with confusion,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that they may seek your name, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V17">
    17
  </span>
  Let them be disappointed and dismayed forever.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yes, let them be confounded and perish;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA83V18">
    18
  </span>
  that they may know that you alone, whose name is Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  are the Most High over all the earth.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>

### 84

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. On an instrument of Gath. A Psalm by the sons of Korah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V1">
    1
  </span>
  How lovely are your dwellings,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh of Armies!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V2">
    2
  </span>
  My soul longs, and even faints for the courts of Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My heart and my flesh cry out for the living God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V3">
    3
  </span>
  Yes, the sparrow has found a home,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and the swallow a nest for herself, where she may have her young,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  near your altars, Yahweh of Armies, my King, and my God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V4">
    4
  </span>
  Blessed are those who dwell in your house.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They are always praising you.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V5">
    5
  </span>
  Blessed are those whose strength is in you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who have set their hearts on a pilgrimage.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V6">
    6
  </span>
  Passing through the valley of Weeping, they make it a place of springs.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yes, the autumn rain covers it with blessings.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V7">
    7
  </span>
  They go from strength to strength.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Every one of them appears before God in Zion.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V8">
    8
  </span>
  Yahweh, God of Armies, hear my prayer.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Listen, God of Jacob.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V9">
    9
  </span>
  Behold, God our shield,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  look at the face of your anointed.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V10">
    10
  </span>
  For a day in your courts is better than a thousand.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I would rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  than to dwell in the tents of wickedness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V11">
    11
  </span>
  For Yahweh God is a sun and a shield.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh will give grace and glory.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He withholds no good thing from those who walk blamelessly.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA84V12">
    12
  </span>
  Yahweh of Armies,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  blessed is the man who trusts in you.
</div>

### 85

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by the sons of Korah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V1">
    1
  </span>
  Yahweh, you have been favorable to your land.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have restored the fortunes of Jacob.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V2">
    2
  </span>
  You have forgiven the iniquity of your people.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have covered all their sin.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V3">
    3
  </span>
  You have taken away all your wrath.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have turned from the fierceness of your anger.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V4">
    4
  </span>
  Turn us, God of our salvation,
</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V5">

  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V6">

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V7">
    7

</div>

</div>

    8

<div class="q2">

</div>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V9">
    9
  </span>
  Surely his salvation is near those who fear him,

<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V10">
    10
  </span>
  Mercy and truth meet together.
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V11">
    11
  </span>
  Truth springs out of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Righteousness has looked down from heaven.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V12">
    12
  </span>
  Yes, Yahweh will give that which is good.
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA85V13">
    13
  </span>

</div>
