### 86

<div class="d">
  A Prayer by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V1">
    1
  </span>
  Hear, Yahweh, and answer me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I am poor and needy.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V2">
    2
  </span>
  Preserve my soul, for I am godly.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You, my God, save your servant who trusts in you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V3">
    3
  </span>
  Be merciful to me, Lord,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I call to you all day long.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V4">
    4
  </span>
  Bring joy to the soul of your servant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for to you, Lord, do I lift up my soul.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V5">
    5
  </span>
  For you, Lord, are good, and ready to forgive,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  abundant in loving kindness to all those who call on you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V6">
    6
  </span>
  Hear, Yahweh, my prayer.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Listen to the voice of my petitions.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V7">
    7
  </span>
  In the day of my trouble I will call on you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you will answer me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V8">
    8
  </span>
  There is no one like you among the gods, Lord,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  nor any deeds like your deeds.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V9">
    9
  </span>
  All nations you have made will come and worship before you, Lord.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They shall glorify your name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V10">
    10
  </span>
  For you are great, and do wondrous things.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You are God alone.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V11">
    11
  </span>
  Teach me your way, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will walk in your truth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Make my heart undivided to fear your name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V12">
    12
  </span>
  I will praise you, Lord my God, with my whole heart.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will glorify your name forever more.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V13">
    13
  </span>
  For your loving kindness is great toward me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have delivered my soul from the lowest Sheol.
  <a href="#PSA86FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V14">
    14
  </span>
  God, the proud have risen up against me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  A company of violent men have sought after my soul,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and they don’t hold regard for you before them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V15">
    15
  </span>
  But you, Lord, are a merciful and gracious God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  slow to anger, and abundant in loving kindness and truth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V16">
    16
  </span>
  Turn to me, and have mercy on me!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Give your strength to your servant.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Save the son of your servant.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA86V17">
    17
  </span>
  Show me a sign of your goodness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that those who hate me may see it, and be shamed,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because you, Yahweh, have helped me, and comforted me.
</div>

    </span>

### 87

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by the sons of Korah; a Song.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA87V1">
    1
  </span>
  His foundation is in the holy mountains.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA87V2">
    2
  </span>
  Yahweh loves the gates of Zion more than all the dwellings of Jacob.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA87V3">
    3
  </span>
  Glorious things are spoken about you, city of God.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA87V4">
    4
  </span>
  I will record Rahab
  <a href="#PSA87FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Rahab is a reference to Egypt.
    </span>
  </a>
  and Babylon among those who acknowledge me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Behold, Philistia, Tyre, and also Ethiopia:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “This one was born there.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA87V5">
    5
  </span>
  Yes, of Zion it will be said, “This one and that one was born in her;”
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the Most High himself will establish her.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA87V6">
    6
  </span>
  Yahweh will count, when he writes up the peoples,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “This one was born there.”
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA87V7">
    7
  </span>
  Those who sing as well as those who dance say,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “All my springs are in you.”
</div>

### 88

<div class="d">
  A Song. A Psalm by the sons of Korah. For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “The Suffering of Affliction.” A contemplation by Heman, the Ezrahite.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V1">
    1
  </span>
  Yahweh, the God of my salvation,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have cried day and night before you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V2">
    2
  </span>
  Let my prayer enter into your presence.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Turn your ear to my cry.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V3">
    3
  </span>
  For my soul is full of troubles.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My life draws near to Sheol.
  <a href="#PSA88FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V4">
    4
  </span>
  I am counted among those who go down into the pit.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I am like a man who has no help,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V5">
    5
  </span>
  set apart among the dead,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  like the slain who lie in the grave,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  whom you remember no more.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They are cut off from your hand.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V6">
    6
  </span>
  You have laid me in the lowest pit,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in the darkest depths.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V7">
    7
  </span>
  Your wrath lies heavily on me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have afflicted me with all your waves.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V8">
    8
  </span>
  You have taken my friends from me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You have made me an abomination to them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I am confined, and I can’t escape.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V9">
    9
  </span>
  My eyes are dim from grief.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have called on you daily, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have spread out my hands to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V10">
    10
  </span>
  Do you show wonders to the dead?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Do the departed spirits rise up and praise you?
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V11">
    11
  </span>
  Is your loving kindness declared in the grave?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Or your faithfulness in Destruction?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V12">
    12
  </span>
  Are your wonders made known in the dark?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Or your righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V13">
    13
  </span>
  But to you, Yahweh, I have cried.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In the morning, my prayer comes before you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V14">
    14
  </span>
  Yahweh, why do you reject my soul?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Why do you hide your face from me?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V15">
    15
  </span>
  I am afflicted and ready to die from my youth up.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  While I suffer your terrors, I am distracted.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V16">
    16
  </span>
  Your fierce wrath has gone over me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your terrors have cut me off.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V17">
    17
  </span>
  They came around me like water all day long.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They completely engulfed me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA88V18">
    18
  </span>
  You have put lover and friend far from me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and my friends into darkness.
</div>

<div class="d">

### 90

<div class="ms">
  BOOK 4
</div>
<div class="d">
  A Prayer by Moses, the man of God.
  <a href="#PSA90FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      The Hebrew word rendered “God” is “אֱלֹהִ֑ים” (Elohim).
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V1">
    1
  </span>
  Lord,
  <a href="#PSA90FN2" class="notemark">
    ‡
    <span class="popup">
      The word translated “Lord” is “Adonai.”
    </span>
  </a>
  you have been our dwelling place for all generations.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V2">
    2
  </span>
  Before the mountains were born,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  before you had formed the earth and the world,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  even from everlasting to everlasting, you are God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V3">
    3
  </span>
  You turn man to destruction, saying,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “Return, you children of men.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V4">
    4
  </span>
  For a thousand years in your sight are just like yesterday when it is past,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  like a watch in the night.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V5">
    5
  </span>
  You sweep them away as they sleep.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In the morning they sprout like new grass.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V6">
    6
  </span>
  In the morning it sprouts and springs up.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  By evening, it is withered and dry.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V7">
    7
  </span>
  For we are consumed in your anger.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  We are troubled in your wrath.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V8">
    8
  </span>
  You have set our iniquities before you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  our secret sins in the light of your presence.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V9">
    9
  </span>
  For all our days have passed away in your wrath.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  We bring our years to an end as a sigh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V10">
    10
  </span>
  The days of our years are seventy,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  or even by reason of strength eighty years;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  yet their pride is but labor and sorrow,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for it passes quickly, and we fly away.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V11">
    11
  </span>
  Who knows the power of your anger,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  your wrath according to the fear that is due to you?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V12">
    12
  </span>
  So teach us to count our days,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that we may gain a heart of wisdom.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V13">
    13
  </span>
  Relent, Yahweh!
  <a href="#PSA90FN3" class="notemark">
    §
    <span class="popup">
      “Yahweh” is God’s proper Name, sometimes rendered “LORD” (all caps) in other translations.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q2">
  How long?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Have compassion on your servants!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V14">
    14
  </span>
  Satisfy us in the morning with your loving kindness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that we may rejoice and be glad all our days.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V15">
    15
  </span>
  Make us glad for as many days as you have afflicted us,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for as many years as we have seen evil.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V16">
    16
  </span>
  Let your work appear to your servants,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  your glory to their children.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA90V17">
    17
  </span>
  Let the favor of the Lord our God be on us.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Establish the work of our hands for us.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yes, establish the work of our hands.
</div>

### 91

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V1">
    1
  </span>
  He who dwells in the secret place of the Most High
</div>
<div class="q2">
  will rest in the shadow of the Almighty.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V2">
    2
  </span>
  I will say of Yahweh, “He is my refuge and my fortress;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my God, in whom I trust.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V3">
    3
  </span>
  For he will deliver you from the snare of the fowler,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and from the deadly pestilence.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V4">
    4
  </span>
  He will cover you with his feathers.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Under his wings you will take refuge.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His faithfulness is your shield and rampart.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V5">
    5
  </span>
  You shall not be afraid of the terror by night,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  nor of the arrow that flies by day,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V6">
    6
  </span>
  nor of the pestilence that walks in darkness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  nor of the destruction that wastes at noonday.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V7">
    7
  </span>
  A thousand may fall at your side,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and ten thousand at your right hand;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but it will not come near you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V8">
    8
  </span>
  You will only look with your eyes,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and see the recompense of the wicked.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V9">
    9
  </span>
  Because you have made Yahweh your refuge,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and the Most High your dwelling place,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V10">
    10
  </span>
  no evil shall happen to you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither shall any plague come near your dwelling.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V11">
    11
  </span>
  For he will put his angels in charge of you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to guard you in all your ways.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V12">
    12
  </span>
  They will bear you up in their hands,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so that you won’t dash your foot against a stone.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V13">
    13
  </span>
  You will tread on the lion and cobra.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You will trample the young lion and the serpent underfoot.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V14">
    14
  </span>
  “Because he has set his love on me, therefore I will deliver him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will set him on high, because he has known my name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V15">
    15
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will be with him in trouble.
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA91V16">
    16
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

### 92

<div class="d">
  A Psalm. A song for the Sabbath day.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V1">
    1
  </span>
  It is a good thing to give thanks to Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to sing praises to your name, Most High,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V2">
    2
  </span>
  to proclaim your loving kindness in the morning,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and your faithfulness every night,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V3">
    3
  </span>
  with the ten-stringed lute, with the harp,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and with the melody of the lyre.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V4">
    4
  </span>
  For you, Yahweh, have made me glad through your work.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will triumph in the works of your hands.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V5">
    5
  </span>
  How great are your works, Yahweh!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your thoughts are very deep.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V6">
    6
  </span>
  A senseless man doesn’t know,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither does a fool understand this:
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V7">
    7
  </span>
  though the wicked spring up as the grass,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and all the evildoers flourish,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  they will be destroyed forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V8">
    8
  </span>
  But you, Yahweh, are on high forever more.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V9">
    9
  </span>
  For behold, your enemies, Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for behold, your enemies shall perish.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All the evildoers will be scattered.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V10">
    10
  </span>
  But you have exalted my horn like that of the wild ox.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I am anointed with fresh oil.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V11">
    11
  </span>
  My eye has also seen my enemies.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My ears have heard of the wicked enemies who rise up against me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V12">
    12
  </span>
  The righteous shall flourish like the palm tree.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He will grow like a cedar in Lebanon.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V13">
    13
  </span>
  They are planted in Yahweh’s house.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They will flourish in our God’s courts.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V14">
    14
  </span>
  They will still produce fruit in old age.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They will be full of sap and green,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA92V15">
    15
  </span>
  to show that Yahweh is upright.
</div>
<div class="q">
  He is my rock,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and there is no unrighteousness in him.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>

<div class="q">

  </span>

    3

  </span>

    9
  </span>

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA94V10">
    10
  </span>

</div>

</div>

    11
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  that they are futile.
</div>

  </span>

<div class="q2">
  and teach out of your law,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA94V13">
    13
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA94V14">
    14
  </span>
  For Yahweh won’t reject his people,
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">

    15
  </span>

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA94V16">
    16
  </span>

</div>

  </span>

</div>

### 97

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V1">
    1
  </span>
  Yahweh reigns!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the earth rejoice!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the multitude of islands be glad!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V2">
    2
  </span>
  Clouds and darkness are around him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Righteousness and justice are the foundation of his throne.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V3">
    3
  </span>
  A fire goes before him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and burns up his adversaries on every side.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V4">
    4
  </span>
  His lightning lights up the world.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The earth sees, and trembles.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V5">
    5
  </span>
  The mountains melt like wax at the presence of Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  at the presence of the Lord of the whole earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V6">
    6
  </span>
  The heavens declare his righteousness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All the peoples have seen his glory.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V7">
    7
  </span>
  Let all them be shamed who serve engraved images,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who boast in their idols.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Worship him, all you gods!
  <a href="#PSA97FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      LXX reads “angels” instead of “gods”.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V8">
    8
  </span>
  Zion heard and was glad.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The daughters of Judah rejoiced
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because of your judgments, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V9">
    9
  </span>
  For you, Yahweh, are most high above all the earth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You are exalted far above all gods.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V10">
    10
  </span>
  You who love Yahweh, hate evil!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He preserves the souls of his saints.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He delivers them out of the hand of the wicked.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V11">
    11
  </span>
  Light is sown for the righteous,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and gladness for the upright in heart.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA97V12">
    12
  </span>
  Be glad in Yahweh, you righteous people!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Give thanks to his holy Name.
</div>

### 98

<div class="d">
  A Psalm.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA98V1">
    1
  </span>
  Sing to Yahweh a new song,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for he has done marvelous things!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His right hand and his holy arm have worked salvation for him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA98V2">
    2
  </span>
  Yahweh has made known his salvation.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He has openly shown his righteousness in the sight of the nations.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA98V3">
    3
  </span>
  He has remembered his loving kindness and his faithfulness toward the house of Israel.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All the ends of the earth have seen the salvation of our God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA98V4">
    4
  </span>
  Make a joyful noise to Yahweh, all the earth!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Burst out and sing for joy, yes, sing praises!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA98V5">
    5
  </span>
  Sing praises to Yahweh with the harp,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  with the harp and the voice of melody.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA98V6">
    6
  </span>
  With trumpets and sound of the ram’s horn,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  make a joyful noise before the King, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA98V7">
    7
  </span>
  Let the sea roar with its fullness;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the world, and those who dwell therein.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA98V8">
    8
  </span>
  Let the rivers clap their hands.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the mountains sing for joy together.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA98V9">
    9
  </span>
  Let them sing before Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for he comes to judge the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  He will judge the world with righteousness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and the peoples with equity.
</div>

### 101

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA101V1">
    1
  </span>
  I will sing of loving kindness and justice.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  To you, Yahweh, I will sing praises.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA101V2">
    2
  </span>
  I will be careful to live a blameless life.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  When will you come to me?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will walk within my house with a blameless heart.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA101V3">
    3
  </span>
  I will set no vile thing before my eyes.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I hate the deeds of faithless men.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They will not cling to me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA101V4">
    4
  </span>
  A perverse heart will be far from me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will have nothing to do with evil.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA101V5">
    5
  </span>
  I will silence whoever secretly slanders his neighbor.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I won’t tolerate one who is arrogant and conceited.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA101V6">
    6
  </span>
  My eyes will be on the faithful of the land,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that they may dwell with me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  He who walks in a perfect way,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  he will serve me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA101V7">
    7
  </span>
  He who practices deceit won’t dwell within my house.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He who speaks falsehood won’t be established before my eyes.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA101V8">
    8
  </span>
  Morning by morning, I will destroy all the wicked of the land,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to cut off all the workers of iniquity from Yahweh’s city.
</div>

### 102

<div class="d">
  A Prayer of the afflicted, when he is overwhelmed and pours out his complaint before Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V1">
    1
  </span>
  Hear my prayer, Yahweh!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let my cry come to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V2">
    2
  </span>
  Don’t hide your face from me in the day of my distress.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Turn your ear to me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Answer me quickly in the day when I call.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V3">
    3
  </span>
  For my days consume away like smoke.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My bones are burned as a torch.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V4">
    4
  </span>
  My heart is blighted like grass, and withered,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I forget to eat my bread.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V5">
    5
  </span>
  By reason of the voice of my groaning,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my bones stick to my skin.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V6">
    6
  </span>
  I am like a pelican of the wilderness.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have become as an owl of the waste places.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V7">
    7
  </span>
  I watch, and have become like a sparrow that is alone on the housetop.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V8">
    8
  </span>
  My enemies reproach me all day.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Those who are mad at me use my name as a curse.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V9">
    9
  </span>
  For I have eaten ashes like bread,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and mixed my drink with tears,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V10">
    10
  </span>
  because of your indignation and your wrath;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you have taken me up and thrown me away.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V11">
    11
  </span>
  My days are like a long shadow.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I have withered like grass.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V12">
    12
  </span>
  But you, Yahweh, will remain forever;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  your renown endures to all generations.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V13">
    13
  </span>
  You will arise and have mercy on Zion,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for it is time to have pity on her.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yes, the set time has come.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V14">
    14
  </span>
  For your servants take pleasure in her stones,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and have pity on her dust.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V15">
    15
  </span>
  So the nations will fear Yahweh’s name,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  all the kings of the earth your glory.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V16">
    16
  </span>
  For Yahweh has built up Zion.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He has appeared in his glory.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V17">
    17
  </span>
  He has responded to the prayer of the destitute,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and has not despised their prayer.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V18">
    18
  </span>
  This will be written for the generation to come.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  A people which will be created will praise Yah,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V19">
    19
  </span>
  for he has looked down from the height of his sanctuary.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  From heaven, Yahweh saw the earth,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V20">
    20
  </span>
  to hear the groans of the prisoner,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to free those who are condemned to death,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V21">
    21
  </span>
  that men may declare Yahweh’s name in Zion,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and his praise in Jerusalem,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V22">
    22
  </span>
  when the peoples are gathered together,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the kingdoms, to serve Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V23">
    23
  </span>
  He weakened my strength along the course.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He shortened my days.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V24">
    24
  </span>
  I said, “My God, don’t take me away in the middle of my days.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your years are throughout all generations.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V25">
    25
  </span>
  Of old, you laid the foundation of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The heavens are the work of your hands.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V26">
    26
  </span>
  They will perish, but you will endure.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yes, all of them will wear out like a garment.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You will change them like a cloak, and they will be changed.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V27">
    27
  </span>
  But you are the same.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your years will have no end.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA102V28">
    28
  </span>
  The children of your servants will continue.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Their offspring will be established before you.”
</div>

  <hr/>

### 103

<div class="d">
  By David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V1">
    1
  </span>
  Praise Yahweh, my soul!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All that is within me, praise his holy name!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V2">
    2
  </span>
  Praise Yahweh, my soul,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and don’t forget all his benefits,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V3">
    3
  </span>
  who forgives all your sins,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who heals all your diseases,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V4">
    4
  </span>
  who redeems your life from destruction,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who crowns you with loving kindness and tender mercies,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V5">
    5
  </span>
  who satisfies your desire with good things,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so that your youth is renewed like the eagle’s.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V6">
    6
  </span>
  Yahweh executes righteous acts,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and justice for all who are oppressed.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V7">
    7
  </span>
  He made known his ways to Moses,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  his deeds to the children of Israel.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V8">
    8
  </span>
  Yahweh is merciful and gracious,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  slow to anger, and abundant in loving kindness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V9">
    9
  </span>
  He will not always accuse;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither will he stay angry forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V10">
    10
  </span>
  He has not dealt with us according to our sins,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  nor repaid us for our iniquities.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V11">
    11
  </span>
  For as the heavens are high above the earth,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so great is his loving kindness toward those who fear him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V12">
    12
  </span>
  As far as the east is from the west,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so far has he removed our transgressions from us.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V13">
    13
  </span>
  Like a father has compassion on his children,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so Yahweh has compassion on those who fear him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V14">
    14
  </span>
  For he knows how we are made.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He remembers that we are dust.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V15">
    15
  </span>
  As for man, his days are like grass.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  As a flower of the field, so he flourishes.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V16">
    16
  </span>
  For the wind passes over it, and it is gone.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Its place remembers it no more.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V17">
    17
  </span>
  But Yahweh’s loving kindness is from everlasting to everlasting with those who fear him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  his righteousness to children’s children,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V18">
    18
  </span>
  to those who keep his covenant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to those who remember to obey his precepts.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V19">
    19
  </span>
  Yahweh has established his throne in the heavens.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His kingdom rules over all.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V20">
    20
  </span>
  Praise Yahweh, you angels of his,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who are mighty in strength, who fulfill his word,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  obeying the voice of his word.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V21">
    21
  </span>
  Praise Yahweh, all you armies of his,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  you servants of his, who do his pleasure.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA103V22">
    22
  </span>
  Praise Yahweh, all you works of his,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in all places of his dominion.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Praise Yahweh, my soul!
</div>

### 104

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V1">
    1
  </span>
  Bless Yahweh, my soul.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh, my God, you are very great.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You are clothed with honor and majesty.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V2">
    2
  </span>
  He covers himself with light as with a garment.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He stretches out the heavens like a curtain.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V3">
    3
  </span>
  He lays the beams of his rooms in the waters.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He makes the clouds his chariot.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He walks on the wings of the wind.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V4">
    4
  </span>
  He makes his messengers
  <a href="#PSA104FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      or, angels
    </span>
  </a>
  winds,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and his servants flames of fire.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V5">
    5
  </span>
  He laid the foundations of the earth,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that it should not be moved forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V6">
    6
  </span>
  You covered it with the deep as with a cloak.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The waters stood above the mountains.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V7">
    7
  </span>
  At your rebuke they fled.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  At the voice of your thunder they hurried away.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V8">
    8
  </span>
  The mountains rose,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the valleys sank down,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to the place which you had assigned to them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V9">
    9
  </span>
  You have set a boundary that they may not pass over,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that they don’t turn again to cover the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V10">
    10
  </span>
  He sends springs into the valleys.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They run among the mountains.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V11">
    11
  </span>
  They give drink to every animal of the field.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The wild donkeys quench their thirst.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V12">
    12
  </span>
  The birds of the sky nest by them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They sing among the branches.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V13">
    13
  </span>
  He waters the mountains from his rooms.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The earth is filled with the fruit of your works.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V14">
    14
  </span>
  He causes the grass to grow for the livestock,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and plants for man to cultivate,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that he may produce food out of the earth:
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V15">
    15
  </span>
  wine that makes the heart of man glad,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  oil to make his face to shine,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and bread that strengthens man’s heart.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V16">
    16
  </span>
  Yahweh’s trees are well watered,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the cedars of Lebanon, which he has planted,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V17">
    17
  </span>
  where the birds make their nests.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The stork makes its home in the cypress trees.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V18">
    18
  </span>
  The high mountains are for the wild goats.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The rocks are a refuge for the rock badgers.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V19">
    19
  </span>
  He appointed the moon for seasons.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The sun knows when to set.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V20">
    20
  </span>
  You make darkness, and it is night,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in which all the animals of the forest prowl.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V21">
    21
  </span>
  The young lions roar after their prey,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and seek their food from God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V22">
    22
  </span>
  The sun rises, and they steal away,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and lie down in their dens.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V23">
    23
  </span>
  Man goes out to his work,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to his labor until the evening.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V24">
    24
  </span>
  Yahweh, how many are your works!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In wisdom, you have made them all.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The earth is full of your riches.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V25">
    25
  </span>
  There is the sea, great and wide,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in which are innumerable living things,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  both small and large animals.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V26">
    26
  </span>
  There the ships go,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and leviathan, whom you formed to play there.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V27">
    27
  </span>
  These all wait for you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that you may give them their food in due season.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V28">
    28
  </span>
  You give to them; they gather.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You open your hand; they are satisfied with good.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V29">
    29
  </span>
  You hide your face; they are troubled.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You take away their breath; they die and return to the dust.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V30">
    30
  </span>
  You send out your Spirit and they are created.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You renew the face of the ground.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V31">
    31
  </span>
  Let Yahweh’s glory endure forever.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let Yahweh rejoice in his works.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V32">
    32
  </span>
  He looks at the earth, and it trembles.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He touches the mountains, and they smoke.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V33">
    33
  </span>
  I will sing to Yahweh as long as I live.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will sing praise to my God while I have any being.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V34">
    34
  </span>
  Let my meditation be sweet to him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will rejoice in Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA104V35">
    35
  </span>
  Let sinners be consumed out of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the wicked be no more.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Bless Yahweh, my soul.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Praise Yah!
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
  <p class="f" id="PSA104FN1">
    <span class="notemark">
      †
    </span>
    <a class="notebackref" href="#PSA104V4">
      104:4
    </a>

      or, angels
    </span>
  </p>
  <hr/>
</div>


### 105

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V1">
    1
  </span>
  Give thanks to Yahweh! Call on his name!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Make his doings known among the peoples.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V2">
    2
  </span>
  Sing to him, sing praises to him!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Tell of all his marvelous works.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V3">
    3
  </span>
  Glory in his holy name.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let the heart of those who seek Yahweh rejoice.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V4">
    4
  </span>
  Seek Yahweh and his strength.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Seek his face forever more.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V5">
    5
  </span>
  Remember his marvelous works that he has done:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V6">
    6
  </span>
  you offspring of Abraham, his servant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  you children of Jacob, his chosen ones.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V7">
    7
  </span>
  He is Yahweh, our God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His judgments are in all the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V8">
    8
  </span>
  He has remembered his covenant forever,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the word which he commanded to a thousand generations,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V9">
    9
  </span>
  the covenant which he made with Abraham,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  his oath to Isaac,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V10">
    10
  </span>
  and confirmed it to Jacob for a statute;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to Israel for an everlasting covenant,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V11">
    11
  </span>
  saying, “To you I will give the land of Canaan,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the lot of your inheritance,”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V12">
    12
  </span>
  when they were but a few men in number,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  yes, very few, and foreigners in it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V13">
    13
  </span>
  They went about from nation to nation,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  from one kingdom to another people.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V14">
    14
  </span>
  He allowed no one to do them wrong.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yes, he reproved kings for their sakes,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V15">
    15
  </span>
  “Don’t touch my anointed ones!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Do my prophets no harm!”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V16">
    16
  </span>
  He called for a famine on the land.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He destroyed the food supplies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V17">
    17
  </span>
  He sent a man before them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Joseph was sold for a slave.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V18">
    18
  </span>
  They bruised his feet with shackles.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His neck was locked in irons,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V19">
    19
  </span>
  until the time that his word happened,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and Yahweh’s word proved him true.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V20">
    20
  </span>
  The king sent and freed him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  even the ruler of peoples, and let him go free.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V21">
    21
  </span>
  He made him lord of his house,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and ruler of all of his possessions,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V22">
    22
  </span>
  to discipline his princes at his pleasure,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and to teach his elders wisdom.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V23">
    23
  </span>
  Israel also came into Egypt.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Jacob lived in the land of Ham.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V24">
    24
  </span>
  He increased his people greatly,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and made them stronger than their adversaries.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V25">
    25
  </span>
  He turned their heart to hate his people,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to conspire against his servants.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V26">
    26
  </span>
  He sent Moses, his servant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and Aaron, whom he had chosen.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V27">
    27
  </span>
  They performed miracles among them,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and wonders in the land of Ham.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V28">
    28
  </span>
  He sent darkness, and made it dark.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They didn’t rebel against his words.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V29">
    29
  </span>
  He turned their waters into blood,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and killed their fish.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V30">
    30
  </span>
  Their land swarmed with frogs,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  even in the rooms of their kings.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V31">
    31
  </span>
  He spoke, and swarms of flies came,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and lice in all their borders.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V32">
    32
  </span>
  He gave them hail for rain,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  with lightning in their land.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V33">
    33
  </span>
  He struck their vines and also their fig trees,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and shattered the trees of their country.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V34">
    34
  </span>
  He spoke, and the locusts came
</div>
<div class="q2">
  with the grasshoppers, without number.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V35">
    35
  </span>
  They ate up every plant in their land,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and ate up the fruit of their ground.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V36">
    36
  </span>
  He struck also all the firstborn in their land,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the first fruits of all their manhood.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V37">
    37
  </span>
  He brought them out with silver and gold.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  There was not one feeble person among his tribes.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V38">
    38
  </span>
  Egypt was glad when they departed,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for the fear of them had fallen on them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V39">
    39
  </span>
  He spread a cloud for a covering,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  fire to give light in the night.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V40">
    40
  </span>
  They asked, and he brought quails,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and satisfied them with the bread of the sky.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V41">
    41
  </span>
  He opened the rock, and waters gushed out.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They ran as a river in the dry places.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V42">
    42
  </span>
  For he remembered his holy word,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and Abraham, his servant.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V43">
    43
  </span>
  He brought his people out with joy,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  his chosen with singing.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V44">
    44
  </span>
  He gave them the lands of the nations.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They took the labor of the peoples in possession,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA105V45">
    45
  </span>
  that they might keep his statutes,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and observe his laws.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Praise Yah!
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 106

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V1">
    1
  </span>
  Praise Yahweh!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Give thanks to Yahweh, for he is good,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for his loving kindness endures forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V2">
    2
  </span>
  Who can utter the mighty acts of Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  or fully declare all his praise?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V3">
    3
  </span>
  Blessed are those who keep justice.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Blessed is one who does what is right at all times.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V4">
    4
  </span>
  Remember me, Yahweh, with the favor that you show to your people.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Visit me with your salvation,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V5">
    5
  </span>
  that I may see the prosperity of your chosen,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that I may rejoice in the gladness of your nation,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that I may glory with your inheritance.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V6">
    6
  </span>
  We have sinned with our fathers.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  We have committed iniquity.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  We have done wickedly.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V7">
    7
  </span>
  Our fathers didn’t understand your wonders in Egypt.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They didn’t remember the multitude of your loving kindnesses,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but were rebellious at the sea, even at the Red Sea.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V8">
    8
  </span>
  Nevertheless he saved them for his name’s sake,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that he might make his mighty power known.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V9">
    9
  </span>
  He rebuked the Red Sea also, and it was dried up;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so he led them through the depths, as through a desert.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V10">
    10
  </span>
  He saved them from the hand of him who hated them,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V11">
    11
  </span>
  The waters covered their adversaries.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  There was not one of them left.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V12">
    12
  </span>
  Then they believed his words.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They sang his praise.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V13">
    13
  </span>
  They soon forgot his works.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They didn’t wait for his counsel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V14">
    14
  </span>
  but gave in to craving in the desert,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and tested God in the wasteland.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V15">
    15
  </span>
  He gave them their request,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but sent leanness into their soul.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V16">
    16
  </span>
  They envied Moses also in the camp,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and Aaron, Yahweh’s saint.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V17">
    17
  </span>
  The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and covered the company of Abiram.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V18">
    18
  </span>
  A fire was kindled in their company.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The flame burned up the wicked.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V19">
    19
  </span>
  They made a calf in Horeb,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and worshiped a molten image.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V20">
    20
  </span>
  Thus they exchanged their glory
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for an image of a bull that eats grass.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V21">
    21
  </span>
  They forgot God, their Savior,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who had done great things in Egypt,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V22">
    22
  </span>
  wondrous works in the land of Ham,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and awesome things by the Red Sea.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V23">
    23
  </span>
  Therefore he said that he would destroy them,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  had Moses, his chosen, not stood before him in the breach,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to turn away his wrath, so that he wouldn’t destroy them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V24">
    24
  </span>
  Yes, they despised the pleasant land.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They didn’t believe his word,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V25">
    25
  </span>
  but murmured in their tents,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and didn’t listen to Yahweh’s voice.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V26">
    26
  </span>
  Therefore he swore to them
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that he would overthrow them in the wilderness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V27">
    27
  </span>
  that he would overthrow their offspring among the nations,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and scatter them in the lands.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V28">
    28
  </span>
  They joined themselves also to Baal Peor,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and ate the sacrifices of the dead.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V29">
    29
  </span>
  Thus they provoked him to anger with their deeds.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The plague broke in on them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V30">
    30
  </span>
  Then Phinehas stood up and executed judgment,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so the plague was stopped.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V31">
    31
  </span>
  That was credited to him for righteousness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for all generations to come.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V32">
    32
  </span>
  They angered him also at the waters of Meribah,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so that Moses was troubled for their sakes;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V33">
    33
  </span>
  because they were rebellious against his spirit,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  he spoke rashly with his lips.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V34">
    34
  </span>
  They didn’t destroy the peoples,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  as Yahweh commanded them,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V35">
    35
  </span>
  but mixed themselves with the nations,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and learned their works.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V36">
    36
  </span>
  They served their idols,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  which became a snare to them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V37">
    37
  </span>
  Yes, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters to demons.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V38">
    38
  </span>
  They shed innocent blood,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  even the blood of their sons and of their daughters,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The land was polluted with blood.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V39">
    39
  </span>
  Thus they were defiled with their works,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and prostituted themselves in their deeds.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V40">
    40
  </span>
  Therefore Yahweh burned with anger against his people.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He abhorred his inheritance.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V41">
    41
  </span>
  He gave them into the hand of the nations.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Those who hated them ruled over them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V42">
    42
  </span>
  Their enemies also oppressed them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They were brought into subjection under their hand.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V43">
    43
  </span>
  He rescued them many times,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but they were rebellious in their counsel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and were brought low in their iniquity.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V44">
    44
  </span>
  Nevertheless he regarded their distress,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  when he heard their cry.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V45">
    45
  </span>
  He remembered for them his covenant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and repented according to the multitude of his loving kindnesses.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V46">
    46
  </span>
  He made them also to be pitied
</div>
<div class="q2">
  by all those who carried them captive.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V47">
    47
  </span>
  Save us, Yahweh, our God,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  gather us from among the nations,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to give thanks to your holy name,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to triumph in your praise!
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA106V48">
    48
  </span>
  Blessed be Yahweh, the God of Israel,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  from everlasting even to everlasting!
</div>
<div class="q">
  Let all the people say, “Amen.”
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Praise Yah!
</div>

### 108

<div class="d">
  A Song. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V1">
    1
  </span>
  My heart is steadfast, God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will sing and I will make music with my soul.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V2">
    2
  </span>
  Wake up, harp and lyre!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will wake up the dawn.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V3">
    3
  </span>
  I will give thanks to you, Yahweh, among the nations.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will sing praises to you among the peoples.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V4">
    4
  </span>
  For your loving kindness is great above the heavens.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your faithfulness reaches to the skies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V5">
    5
  </span>
  Be exalted, God, above the heavens!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let your glory be over all the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V6">
    6
  </span>
  That your beloved may be delivered,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  save with your right hand, and answer us.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V7">
    7
  </span>
  God has spoken from his sanctuary: “In triumph,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will divide Shechem, and measure out the valley of Succoth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V8">
    8
  </span>
  Gilead is mine. Manasseh is mine.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Ephraim also is my helmet.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Judah is my scepter.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V9">
    9
  </span>
  Moab is my wash pot.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will toss my sandal on Edom.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will shout over Philistia.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V10">
    10
  </span>
  Who will bring me into the fortified city?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Who will lead me to Edom?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V11">
    11
  </span>
  Haven’t you rejected us, God?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You don’t go out, God, with our armies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V12">
    12
  </span>
  Give us help against the enemy,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for the help of man is vain.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA108V13">
    13
  </span>
  Through God, we will do valiantly,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for it is he who will tread down our enemies.
</div>

  <hr/>

### 109

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V1">
    1
  </span>
  God of my praise, don’t remain silent,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V2">
    2
  </span>
  for they have opened the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of deceit against me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They have spoken to me with a lying tongue.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V3">
    3
  </span>
  They have also surrounded me with words of hatred,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and fought against me without a cause.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V4">
    4
  </span>
  In return for my love, they are my adversaries;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but I am in prayer.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V5">
    5
  </span>
  They have rewarded me evil for good,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and hatred for my love.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V6">
    6
  </span>
  Set a wicked man over him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let an adversary stand at his right hand.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V7">
    7
  </span>
  When he is judged, let him come out guilty.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let his prayer be turned into sin.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V8">
    8
  </span>
  Let his days be few.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let another take his office.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V9">
    9
  </span>
  Let his children be fatherless,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and his wife a widow.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V10">
    10
  </span>
  Let his children be wandering beggars.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let them be sought from their ruins.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V11">
    11
  </span>
  Let the creditor seize all that he has.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let strangers plunder the fruit of his labor.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V12">
    12
  </span>
  Let there be no one to extend kindness to him,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  neither let there be anyone to have pity on his fatherless children.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V13">
    13
  </span>
  Let his posterity be cut off.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In the generation following let their name be blotted out.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V14">
    14
  </span>
  Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered by Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t let the sin of his mother be blotted out.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V15">
    15
  </span>
  Let them be before Yahweh continually,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that he may cut off their memory from the earth;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V16">
    16
  </span>
  because he didn’t remember to show kindness,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but persecuted the poor and needy man,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the broken in heart, to kill them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V17">
    17
  </span>
  Yes, he loved cursing, and it came to him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He didn’t delight in blessing, and it was far from him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V18">
    18
  </span>
  He clothed himself also with cursing as with his garment.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  It came into his inward parts like water,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  like oil into his bones.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V19">
    19
  </span>
  Let it be to him as the clothing with which he covers himself,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for the belt that is always around him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V20">
    20
  </span>
  This is the reward of my adversaries from Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  of those who speak evil against my soul.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V21">
    21
  </span>
  But deal with me, Yahweh the Lord,
  <a href="#PSA109FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      The word translated “Lord” is “Adonai.”
    </span>
  </a>
  for your name’s sake,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  because your loving kindness is good, deliver me;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V22">
    22
  </span>
  for I am poor and needy.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My heart is wounded within me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V23">
    23
  </span>
  I fade away like an evening shadow.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I am shaken off like a locust.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V24">
    24
  </span>
  My knees are weak through fasting.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My body is thin and lacks fat.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V25">
    25
  </span>
  I have also become a reproach to them.
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V26">
    26
  </span>
  Help me, Yahweh, my God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Save me according to your loving kindness;
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V27">
    27
  </span>
  that they may know that this is your hand;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that you, Yahweh, have done it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V28">
    28
  </span>
  They may curse, but you bless.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  When they arise, they will be shamed,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but your servant shall rejoice.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V29">
    29
  </span>
  Let my adversaries be clothed with dishonor.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let them cover themselves with their own shame as with a robe.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V30">
    30
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA109V31">
    31
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  to save him from those who judge his soul.

### 110

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA110V1">
    1
  </span>
  Yahweh says to my Lord, “Sit at my right hand,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  until I make your enemies your footstool for your feet.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA110V2">
    2
  </span>
  Yahweh will send out the rod of your strength out of Zion.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Rule among your enemies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA110V3">
    3
  </span>
  Your people offer themselves willingly in the day of your power, in holy array.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Out of the womb of the morning, you have the dew of your youth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA110V4">
    4
  </span>
  Yahweh has sworn, and will not change his mind:
</div>
<div class="q2">
  “You are a priest forever in the order of Melchizedek.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA110V5">
    5
  </span>
  The Lord is at your right hand.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He will crush kings in the day of his wrath.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA110V6">
    6
  </span>
  He will judge among the nations.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He will heap up dead bodies.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He will crush the ruler of the whole earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA110V7">
    7
  </span>
  He will drink of the brook on the way;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  therefore he will lift up his head.
</div>

### 111

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V1">
    1
  </span>
  Praise Yah!
  <a href="#PSA111FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Psalm 111 is an acrostic poem, with each verse after the initial “Praise Yah!” starting with a letter of the alphabet (ordered from Alef to Tav).
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will give thanks to Yahweh with my whole heart,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in the council of the upright, and in the congregation.
</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V2">
    2
  </span>

</div>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V3">
    3
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  His righteousness endures forever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V4">
    4
  </span>
  He has caused his wonderful works to be remembered.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yahweh is gracious and merciful.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V5">
    5
  </span>
  He has given food to those who fear him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He always remembers his covenant.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V6">
    6
  </span>
  He has shown his people the power of his works,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  in giving them the heritage of the nations.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V7">
    7
  </span>
  The works of his hands are truth and justice.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All his precepts are sure.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V8">
    8
  </span>
  They are established forever and ever.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They are done in truth and uprightness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V9">
    9
  </span>
  He has sent redemption to his people.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He has ordained his covenant forever.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His name is holy and awesome!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA111V10">
    10
  </span>
  The fear of Yahweh is the beginning of wisdom.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  All those who do his work have a good understanding.
</div>
<div class="q">
  His praise endures forever!
</div>

### 112

<div class="q">

  </span>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA112V9">
    9
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  His righteousness endures forever.
</div>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA112V10">

  </span>

</div>

### 115

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA115V1">

  </span>

</div>

    5

    6
  </span>

</div>

</div>

</div>

  He is their help and their shield.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA115V12">

  </span>

<div class="q2">
  He will bless the house of Aaron.

  <span class="verse" id="PSA115V13">
    13
  </span>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA115V14">

  </span>

  </span>

  </span>

</div>

    18
  </span>

### 116

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA116V1">
    1
  </span>
