### 138

<div class="d">
  By David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA138V1">
    1
  </span>
  I will give you thanks with my whole heart.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Before the gods,
  <a href="#PSA138FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      The word elohim, used here, usually means “God” but can also mean “gods”, “princes”, or “angels”.
    </span>
  </a>
  I will sing praises to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA138V2">
    2
  </span>
  I will bow down toward your holy temple,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and give thanks to your Name for your loving kindness and for your truth;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you have exalted your Name and your Word above all.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA138V3">
    3
  </span>
  In the day that I called, you answered me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You encouraged me with strength in my soul.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA138V4">
    4
  </span>
  All the kings of the earth will give you thanks, Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for they have heard the words of your mouth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA138V5">
    5
  </span>
  Yes, they will sing of the ways of Yahweh,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for Yahweh’s glory is great!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA138V6">
    6
  </span>
  For though Yahweh is high, yet he looks after the lowly;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but he knows the proud from afar.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA138V7">
    7
  </span>
  Though I walk in the middle of trouble, you will revive me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You will stretch out your hand against the wrath of my enemies.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your right hand will save me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA138V8">
    8
  </span>
  Yahweh will fulfill that which concerns me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your loving kindness, Yahweh, endures forever.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t forsake the works of your own hands.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
  <p class="f" id="PSA138FN1">
    <span class="notemark">
      †
    </span>
    <a class="notebackref" href="#PSA138V1">
      138:1
    </a>
    <span class="ft">
      The word elohim, used here, usually means “God” but can also mean “gods”, “princes”, or “angels”.
    </span>
  </p>
  <hr/>
</div>


### 139

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V1">
    1
  </span>
  Yahweh, you have searched me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and you know me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V2">
    2
  </span>
  You know my sitting down and my rising up.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You perceive my thoughts from afar.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V3">
    3
  </span>
  You search out my path and my lying down,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and are acquainted with all my ways.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V4">
    4
  </span>
  For there is not a word on my tongue,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but behold, Yahweh, you know it altogether.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V5">
    5
  </span>
  You hem me in behind and before.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You laid your hand on me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V6">
    6
  </span>
  This knowledge is beyond me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  It’s lofty.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I can’t attain it.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V7">
    7
  </span>
  Where could I go from your Spirit?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Or where could I flee from your presence?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V8">
    8
  </span>
  If I ascend up into heaven, you are there.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  If I make my bed in Sheol,
  <a href="#PSA139FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </a>
  behold, you are there!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V9">
    9
  </span>
  If I take the wings of the dawn,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and settle in the uttermost parts of the sea,
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V10">
    10
  </span>
  even there your hand will lead me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and your right hand will hold me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V11">
    11
  </span>
  If I say, “Surely the darkness will overwhelm me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The light around me will be night,”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V12">
    12
  </span>
  even the darkness doesn’t hide from you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  but the night shines as the day.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The darkness is like light to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V13">
    13
  </span>
  For you formed my inmost being.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  You knit me together in my mother’s womb.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V14">
    14
  </span>
  I will give thanks to you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I am fearfully and wonderfully made.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Your works are wonderful.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My soul knows that very well.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V15">
    15
  </span>
  My frame wasn’t hidden from you,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  when I was made in secret,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  woven together in the depths of the earth.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V16">
    16
  </span>
  Your eyes saw my body.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In your book they were all written,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the days that were ordained for me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  when as yet there were none of them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V17">
    17
  </span>
  How precious to me are your thoughts, God!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  How vast is their sum!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V18">
    18
  </span>
  If I would count them, they are more in number than the sand.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  When I wake up, I am still with you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V19">
    19
  </span>
  If only you, God, would kill the wicked.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Get away from me, you bloodthirsty men!
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V20">
    20
  </span>
  For they speak against you wickedly.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Your enemies take your name in vain.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V21">
    21
  </span>
  Yahweh, don’t I hate those who hate you?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Am I not grieved with those who rise up against you?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V22">
    22
  </span>
  I hate them with perfect hatred.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They have become my enemies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V23">
    23
  </span>
  Search me, God, and know my heart.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Try me, and know my thoughts.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA139V24">
    24
  </span>
  See if there is any wicked way in me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and lead me in the everlasting way.
</div>

### 140

<div class="d">
  For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V1">
    1
  </span>
  Deliver me, Yahweh, from evil men.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Preserve me from violent men:
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V2">
    2
  </span>
  those who devise mischief in their hearts.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They continually gather themselves together for war.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V3">
    3
  </span>
  They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Viper’s poison is under their lips.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V4">
    4
  </span>
  Yahweh, keep me from the hands of the wicked.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Preserve me from the violent men who have determined to trip my feet.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V5">
    5
  </span>
  The proud have hidden a snare for me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  they have spread the cords of a net by the path.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They have set traps for me.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V6">
    6
  </span>
  I said to Yahweh, “You are my God.”
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Listen to the cry of my petitions, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V7">
    7
  </span>
  Yahweh, the Lord, the strength of my salvation,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  you have covered my head in the day of battle.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V8">
    8
  </span>
  Yahweh, don’t grant the desires of the wicked.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t let their evil plans succeed, or they will become proud.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V9">
    9
  </span>
  As for the head of those who surround me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  let the mischief of their own lips cover them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V10">
    10
  </span>
  Let burning coals fall on them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Let them be thrown into the fire,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  into miry pits, from where they never rise.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V11">
    11
  </span>
  An evil speaker won’t be established in the earth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Evil will hunt the violent man to overthrow him.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V12">
    12
  </span>
  I know that Yahweh will maintain the cause of the afflicted,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and justice for the needy.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA140V13">
    13
  </span>
  Surely the righteous will give thanks to your name.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  The upright will dwell in your presence.
</div>

### 141

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V1">
    1
  </span>
  Yahweh, I have called on you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Come to me quickly!
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Listen to my voice when I call to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V2">
    2
  </span>
  Let my prayer be set before you like incense;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  the lifting up of my hands like the evening sacrifice.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V3">
    3
  </span>
  Set a watch, Yahweh, before my mouth.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Keep the door of my lips.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V4">
    4
  </span>
  Don’t incline my heart to any evil thing,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  to practice deeds of wickedness with men who work iniquity.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t let me eat of their delicacies.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V5">
    5
  </span>
  Let the righteous strike me, it is kindness;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  let him reprove me, it is like oil on the head;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  don’t let my head refuse it;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Yet my prayer is always against evil deeds.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V6">
    6
  </span>
  Their judges are thrown down by the sides of the rock.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  They will hear my words, for they are well spoken.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V7">
    7
  </span>
  “As when one plows and breaks up the earth,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  our bones are scattered at the mouth of Sheol.”
  <a href="#PSA141FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      Sheol is the place of the dead.
    </span>
  </a>
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V8">
    8
  </span>
  For my eyes are on you, Yahweh, the Lord.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I take refuge in you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Don’t leave my soul destitute.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V9">
    9
  </span>
  Keep me from the snare which they have laid for me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  from the traps of the workers of iniquity.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA141V10">
    10
  </span>
  Let the wicked fall together into their own nets
</div>
<div class="q2">
  while I pass by.
</div>

    </span>

### 142

<div class="d">
  A contemplation by David, when he was in the cave. A Prayer.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA142V1">
    1
  </span>
  I cry with my voice to Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  With my voice, I ask Yahweh for mercy.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA142V2">
    2
  </span>
  I pour out my complaint before him.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I tell him my troubles.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA142V3">
    3
  </span>
  When my spirit was overwhelmed within me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  you knew my route.
</div>
<div class="q">
  On the path in which I walk,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  they have hidden a snare for me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA142V4">
    4
  </span>
  Look on my right, and see;
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for there is no one who is concerned for me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Refuge has fled from me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  No one cares for my soul.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA142V5">
    5
  </span>
  I cried to you, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I said, “You are my refuge,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my portion in the land of the living.”
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA142V6">
    6
  </span>
  Listen to my cry,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I am in desperate need.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Deliver me from my persecutors,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for they are too strong for me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA142V7">
    7
  </span>
  Bring my soul out of prison,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  that I may give thanks to your name.
</div>
<div class="q">
  The righteous will surround me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you will be good to me.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 143

<div class="d">
  A Psalm by David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V1">
    1
  </span>
  Hear my prayer, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Listen to my petitions.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In your faithfulness and righteousness, relieve me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V2">
    2
  </span>
  Don’t enter into judgment with your servant,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for in your sight no man living is righteous.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V3">
    3
  </span>
  For the enemy pursues my soul.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He has struck my life down to the ground.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  He has made me live in dark places, as those who have been long dead.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V4">
    4
  </span>
  Therefore my spirit is overwhelmed within me.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My heart within me is desolate.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V5">
    5
  </span>
  I remember the days of old.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I meditate on all your doings.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I contemplate the work of your hands.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V6">
    6
  </span>
  I spread out my hands to you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My soul thirsts for you, like a parched land.
</div>
<div class="qs">
  Selah.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V7">
    7
  </span>
  Hurry to answer me, Yahweh.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  My spirit fails.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Don’t hide your face from me,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  so that I don’t become like those who go down into the pit.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V8">
    8
  </span>
  Cause me to hear your loving kindness in the morning,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I trust in you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Cause me to know the way in which I should walk,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I lift up my soul to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V9">
    9
  </span>
  Deliver me, Yahweh, from my enemies.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I flee to you to hide me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V10">
    10
  </span>
  Teach me to do your will,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for you are my God.
</div>
<div class="q">
  Your Spirit is good.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Lead me in the land of uprightness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V11">
    11
  </span>
  Revive me, Yahweh, for your name’s sake.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  In your righteousness, bring my soul out of trouble.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA143V12">
    12
  </span>
  In your loving kindness, cut off my enemies,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and destroy all those who afflict my soul,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  for I am your servant.
</div>
<div class="footnote">
  <hr/>
</div>


### 144

<div class="d">
  By David.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V1">
    1
  </span>
  Blessed be Yahweh, my rock,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who trains my hands to war,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and my fingers to battle—
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V2">
    2
  </span>
  my loving kindness, my fortress,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my high tower, my deliverer,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  my shield, and he in whom I take refuge,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who subdues my people under me.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V3">
    3
  </span>
  Yahweh, what is man, that you care for him?
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Or the son of man, that you think of him?
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V4">
    4
  </span>
  Man is like a breath.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His days are like a shadow that passes away.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V5">
    5
  </span>
  Part your heavens, Yahweh, and come down.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Touch the mountains, and they will smoke.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V6">
    6
  </span>
  Throw out lightning, and scatter them.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Send out your arrows, and rout them.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V7">
    7
  </span>
  Stretch out your hand from above,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  rescue me, and deliver me out of great waters,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  out of the hands of foreigners,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V8">
    8
  </span>
  whose mouths speak deceit,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  whose right hand is a right hand of falsehood.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V9">
    9
  </span>
  I will sing a new song to you, God.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  On a ten-stringed lyre, I will sing praises to you.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V10">
    10
  </span>
  You are he who gives salvation to kings,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  who rescues David, his servant, from the deadly sword.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V11">
    11
  </span>
  Rescue me, and deliver me out of the hands of foreigners,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  whose mouths speak deceit,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  whose right hand is a right hand of falsehood.
</div>
<div class="b">
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V12">
    12
  </span>
  Then our sons will be like well-nurtured plants,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  our daughters like pillars carved to adorn a palace.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V13">
    13
  </span>
  Our barns are full, filled with all kinds of provision.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Our sheep produce thousands and ten thousands in our fields.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V14">
    14
  </span>
  Our oxen will pull heavy loads.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  There is no breaking in, and no going away,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  and no outcry in our streets.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA144V15">
    15
  </span>
  Happy are the people who are in such a situation.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  Happy are the people whose God is Yahweh.
</div>

### 145

<div class="d">
  A praise psalm by David.
  <a href="#PSA145FN1" class="notemark">
    †
    <span class="popup">
      This is an acrostic psalm, with every verse (including the second half of verse 13) starting with a consecutive letter of the Hebrew alphabet.
    </span>
  </a>

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V1">
    1
  </span>
  I will exalt you, my God, the King.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will praise your name forever and ever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V2">
    2
  </span>
  Every day I will praise you.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will extol your name forever and ever.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V3">
    3
  </span>
  Great is Yahweh, and greatly to be praised!
</div>
<div class="q2">

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V4">
    4
  </span>

<div class="q2">

  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V5">
    5

</div>
<div class="q2">
  on your wondrous works.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V6">
    6
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q2">
  I will declare your greatness.
</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V7">
    7
  </span>

</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V8">
    8
  </span>
  Yahweh is gracious, merciful,
</div>
<div class="q2">
  slow to anger, and of great loving kindness.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V9">
    9
  </span>
  Yahweh is good to all.
</div>
<div class="q2">
  His tender mercies are over all his works.
</div>
<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V10">
    10
  </span>

</div>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA145V11">

  </span>

    12
  </span>

<div class="q">

</div>
<div class="q">
  Yahweh is faithful in all his words,
</div>

  </span>

### 146

<div class="q">
  <span class="verse" id="PSA146V1">
    1
  </span>

    6
  </span>

</div>

    8

  <span class="verse" id="PSA147V14">
    14
  </span>

</div>

</div>

  <span class="verse" id="PSA147V15">
    15

</div>

</div>

    18
